royame perse syde whan departed playn sawe self ouer apperceyued grete plente peple londe myght suffyse ne withstonde yf helde hem gydre ffor fore whan dwellid perse dwellid fer sondre suche wise knewe power whan sawe many meruaillous grete desdayne suffred pryde grieuousnes one prince take counseyl emonge sawe peple myght resiste myght conquere alle londes ther aboute one thynge destrobled kynge thenne dyde manere fonde emonge hondred lignages whiche euerich meyne euery lignage brought forth arowe marked suche wise arowe eche lignage myght knowen whan alle thise arowes brought gydre called lytil chylde commanded hym take vp suche one wolde ffor acorded emonge lignage arowe shold taken vp chylde shold chese kynge chylde toke vp one lignage called selduces knewe lignage muste chese kynge toke hondred prudent wise men coude fynde al lignage commanded eche shold brynge arowe wheron name shold wreton called chylde bad hym take vp one arowes concluded emonge shold kynge toke vp arowe toke vp one whiche wreton selduc selduc moche goodly man gretely honoured lignage grete stronge good knyght wel proued semed wel good man hye werkes chees alle man theyr kynge promysed dyde hym tho partyes capitulo ixo ye haue herd peple cry en deme ned contre thoryent ye may bere crystiente contened ruled partyes world knowe ye certayn tyme fouden fewe drede lord theyr herte alle right wysnesse alle trouthe alle pyte faylled fayth ihesu cryste quenchid charyte men spack debate discordes warres nyhe oueral suche wyse semed thende world nyghe signes lord sayth gospell ffor pestylences famynes grete therthe ferdfulnes heuen tremblyng therthe many place many thinges ought fere hertes men drawe fro euyl brynge remembraunce lord deef blynde heeryng seey g nedeful saue theyr sowles prynces baron brente destroyed contrees theyr neyghbours yf ony man saued ony thynge theyr kepyng theyr owne lordes toke put prison greuous tormentis take fro suche suche wyse chyldren ben riche men men myght see goo fro dore dore begge gete theyr brede somme deye hungre mesease chirches ne religyouses kept theyr priuyleges ne none fraunchyses taken fro alle mocht founden wel meobles rente thynges ye cross chalyces sensours toke fro chirches molt selle yf ony fledde chirche warante saue hym taken drawen vylaynously tauerne place monkes clerkes doon wronges shame myght ther iustyce trespaced ne forfayted nothyng contrees ful theues murdriers cytees ne good townes noman sure regned customably dronkenship lecherye playeng dyse roberyes ther mariage kepte ne lignage also euyl lyf clerkes werse bysshops ne prelate durst reprehende ne chastyse none theyr euyl werkes rente holy chirche gaf ne payd none solde benefice fynably saye yow alle euyl werkes surprysed alle crystiente suche wyse semed eueryche dyde payne serue deuyll bataylle themperour romayne constantynople ayenst puissaunt prynce thoryent named belphet cao xo owr lorde pyte chastyseth world spare wel bete child loueth saue suffred grete flawe come contre chastyse peple ffor tyme whan themperour romayn lord constantynoble yssued partyes thoryent puissant hethen prynce named belphet whiche brought hym grete strengthe brought thempire constantinoble began take waste fode fonde fortress cytees castellis toke al assault ffor nothyng myght resist e smote doun therthe pepl hool fledde fore hym tydynges cam themperour grete lord supprised taken alle contre anon without taryeng sente thempire dyde thene somone hoost assembled moche peple coude gete moche good e myght fine worke grete whan peple wer comen yssued many men arm warre myght haue drewe parte bel cam fonde hym sone ferre entred londe whan knewe eche nygh ordeyned th bataylles fyghte assembled cruelly grete ang peple eche grete hate hen foughte fo tenhaunce theyr lawe tencrece theyr power cristen men defended theyr fayth lawe ihesu criste saue ke e theyr liues franchyses theyr wyues childeren theyr contree bataylle moche grete cruelle moche peple sla n blode shadde atte laste grekes myght suffre e faytes ne grete plente mescreaus f edde discomfyted fowle none retorned agayn ranne awa oute ordenauce euerych myght best saue hym folowed dyde alle wolde slewe many toke grete plente lyue emonge alle themperour taken hym self whan tydinges cam contre batayl loste themperour taken ther grete sorowe alle tholde men wyues childeren ben belphet pryn ce myscreauntes seeyng thus playn victorye cristen men mounted aroos grete pryde ffor thought wel shold fynde barre shold letee hym doo thempyre whan lodged hoost aboute hym comanded themperour brought fore hym taken bataylle sette foote vpon necke themperour dyde ofte whan shold mounte vpon horsbak descende shame despite fayth lord cristen peple whan thus whyle shamed reuyled despyted themperour lete hym goo delyuerd hym som baron prisoner whan themperour come agayn constantynoble baron londe reputed hym ouermoche dishonoured shamefully conduyted bataille toke hym raced eyen lete hym vse lif sorowe shame prynce belphet began take alle londe suche wyse lytil whyle coquerd fro lystes surye vnto see called braas seynt george wel xxx iourneyes lengthe x brede som place xv whan cam braas wold haue passed constantinoble whiche side litil see myght finde shippis ynowgh thus cristen peple londe theyr synnes vnder cruell peple emong noble hye cyte saynt peter made fyrst chyef cristente antioche taken ende subgette vnto turkes thus belphet seygnorye demayne londes named celessurye two cilices pamphylee lyce lycarne cappadoce galace bethuye parte lasse asye thise coutrees ar moch fertile ful peple hethen peple began bete chirches greue cristen peple plesyd ffor grete affraye drede hertes cristen peple fledde vj iourneyes fro said belphet thynge greuyd merueylously holy cyte iherusalem peple coutre ffor whyles themperour constantynoble good pee grete power many grete socours grete comfort ryche yeftes large almesses cam vnto peple surye also fro londe antioche thenne loste alle none hope euer ony ayde ne socours shold come wherfor supposed euer seruage captyuite without ony rauson many maners tormens cristen peple suffred theyr synnes tyme capitulo xjo whyles tyme peryllous seygnorye thyse hethen men cam oftymes pylgremages grekes latyns iherusalem ffor praye oure lord crye hym mercy wold forgete thus peple yet many cam theder grete perylle ffor alle countrees whiche shold passe ful theyr enemyes ofte robbed slayn whan myght escape come holy cyte myght entre therin eche persone muste paye besaunt trybute wherof happed ofte despoylled wherof myght paye trybute myght entre town suffred colde hungre grete mesease many deyde herof casten men town moche greued susteyned lyued muste burye dede sec e thyng nedeful self myght entre town yet greued ffor som murdred holy place cyte secretely doon moche repreef openly ther fyl caste theyr visage spytte myddes theyr visage som men bette w erfore cristen men town som acqueyntauces hethen men conduyted ladde th th yr p lgremages kepe theyr power cyte malfe cyte puye l chirche n med saynte marye de la latyne whereby hospital ou e peple chappel named saynt iohn l mont saynt iohan patriark andr chirche lady cure hospital pourchassed alle nede ul receyuyd alle pour pylgryms whiche w erof yue hows moche gre e cha yte thus f ccisten peple grete disease toun nothyng displesyd whan made theyr deuocion holy place toun grete traueylles grete co e whan seruyse lord hethen cam grete noyse crye satte vpon aulce threwe doun chalyces brake lampes tapres yet angre cristen peple toke ofte patriarke ne herde eer threwe hym grounde defowled hym vnder theyr foot whiche alle grete sorowe moche pyte thyse owes meseases cristen men londe r e haue sayd fore cccc four score ten yere alwey cryed vnto lord mercy syghes treres prayde hym deuoutly wold alle forgete good lord aftir tempeste derke weder wel brynge clerenes fayr season behelde peple pyte sente comforte delyuerance tormentes whiche longe ben aftir ben four cccclxxxx yere seruage hethen peple lord pourueyed remedye cristen peple capitulo xij haue wel said byfore many londes cam pilgryme ihrlm emong ther one royame ffrance born bisshopprych amyens one named peter whiche ben heremyte wode therfor called peter theremyte litil man body persone despite lytil preysed semblaunt merueyllous grete herte moche clere engyne good vnderstondyng spak right wel whan cam gate iherusalem payd trybute besaut entred cyte lodged good cristen man hows petre alwey enquyred demauded moche hoost gouernaunce estate cyte cristen men conteyned vnder hethen men theyr lord demened gouerned hoost whiche longe ben towne tolde hym alle maner playnly tymes passyd cristent defowled holy place dishonoured whiche sorouful hym self good town doo pylgremage sawe wel perceyued grete partye caityfnes cristen men herd saye patriarke good wyse man deuote religyo named symeon peter thought wold goo speke hym demande hym estate chirches clergye peple cam hym dyde though asked hym alle thise thynges patriarke apperceyued wel wordes coutinaunce man dredde god right wyse vnderstondyng began telle hym layser alle meseases cristen peple whan peter herde thise sorowes mouthe good man byleuyd wel coude absteyne hym fro grete syghes wepyng many teeres pyte ofte maded patriarke yf ther ony coseil remedye werke holy deuote patriarke answerd hym haue made many orysons prayer vnto oure lord god receyue v mercy grace apperceyue wel synnes yet purged ffor ben certaynly culpe blame whan oure lord whiche rightwys holdeth v yet payne renome contrees yonde montaynes moche grete peple specially ffraunce ben good cristen peple moche stedfaste fayth therfor oure lord holdeth day moche grete pea hye puissance yf wold praye lord wolde haue pyte v toke counseyl socoure v haue certaynly hope lord shold helpe v taccomplysshe oure werke ffor ye see wel grekes themperour constantinoble whiche ben neyghbours kynnesmen maye helpe ne counseyle v ffor self ben sayth destroyed haue power defende theyr owne lande whan peter herd answerd maner fayr fader trouthe ye haue sayd ffor londe god thanked fayth oure lord moche better holden kepte ony londes haue ben syth departed iourneye fro contre byleue certaynly mescase seruage whiche thise hethen mysbyleuyd peple holde inne playsyre almyghty god theyr good wylles shold fynde couseyl ayde grete nede werke wherfor counseyl one thyng yf aggreable seme good ye sende lettres vnto oure holy fader pope chirche rome vnto kynges prynces baron occident weste parte late wete playnly ye crye mercy wolde socoure loue god fayth suche maner myght haue honoure world sauacon soules ye pour peple ye haue nede make grete dispecis yf ye thynke sufficiaunt grete message ffor loue ihu criste remyssyon synnes shal entreprise vyage offre self take moche traueyl promyse truly shal late haue knowleche yf god sende grace come thydre whan patriarke herd moche grete ioye sente anon moost saddest wysest men cristen pepl clerkes laye men sayde shewde bounte seruyse good man offryd right glad thanked hym moche thenne anon withoute taryenge made theyr wrytynges sealed theyr seales delyuerd peter theremyte said peter theremyte entreprised hardyly vyage thapparicon vision sawe sleep ca xiijo truly lord god swete pyteous mercyful ffor wylle suffre perysshe ne loste haue hym ferme stedfast hope whan men lacke helpe god sendeth ayde may clerely seen werke fro whens cometh pour man whiche lytil despysed persone wery brused grete iourneye waye durste enterprise grete dede werke myght wene lord wolde accomplysshe grete werke hym dylyure peple fro myserye caytyfnes ben nygh fyue c yere hardynesse cam hym grete charyte hym fayth wrought hym loue bretheren thise dayes happed thynge moche lyft vp herte poursue enterprise ffor good man whan taken message charge therof wente moche ofter woonte doo holy place cyte cam euentide chirche holy sepulchre made prayer deuoutly grete plente teeris aftir sleepte vpon pamente hym semed saueour ihesu criste cam fore hym charged hym self doo message said hym petre aryse vp hastely goo surely thedyr thou hast entreprysed ffor shal tyme hen forth holy cyte clensed peple socoured petre awoke poynt fro forthon abandouned vnto waye also sure iourneye message doon entermed appoynted departyng doo erande leue benediction patriarke thempyre suche customme ronne grete whyle whan prelate deed e rynges cro brought themperour gaf clerkes chapylayns wolde sente chyrches bad shoolde holde theyr bisshops archebisshops without election ther proef whiche holy chirche adommaged sore sente ofte persones propice therto pope grego sawe customme ayenst right lawe also ayenst reason prayd hym amyably leue loue god holy chirche sauacion lord contre robert dyde vnto holy fader peple moche honour servyse bounce wold take yet laste holy fader wente hym salerne becam seke laye doun deyde buryed cardynals chose another whiche named viator whiche endured one moneth aboutes hym choos vrban spack fore vrban sawe themperour yet ce angre durst abandone hym ne put hym power helde hym forteresses baron goddes sake retryned hym grete doubte pylgremage grete men enterprised assone wynter passed wold putte pylgremage mene peple knyghtes barous aftir acqueynted one sente eche lettres message taccorde goo gydre apoynted tyme departyng waye sholde holde whan marche come ye sholde haue seen horse arrayed sommyers palfroyes stedes tentes pauyllons make armures ye maye wel knowe moche doo many thynges ffor baron acorded shold goo alle gydre ffor contre myght suffyse ne fynde shold nedeful ffor whiche cause alle hoostes neuyr assembled ye shal tyl cam vnto cyte nycene mene peple charged self moche tentes ne armures ffor myght bere therfor euery man garnysshid hym aftir moneye goodes moche supposed shold nedeful hym whan daye departyng cam ther grete sorowes grete wepynges grete cryes departyng pylgryms ffor fewe howses som wente suche howsholders ther wente alle caryed theyr wyues bare theyr childer n merueyllous thynge see meuynges ffor byfore acustomed see suche thynges fraunce ne neuer byfore crosse born ne taken pylgremage thauentures rowte cristen men viage whome one gaultyer withoute knowleche captayne capitulo xviijo yere thyncarnacion lord four score xvj eght daye marche cam gentilman knyght right noble named gaultier without knowleche surname hym cam merueyllous grete plente folke foot ffor ther fewe men hors bak rowte passed allemayne drewe hem toward hongrye royamme hongrye alle enuyronned grete water large mers depe lake suche wyse none myght entre ne yssue certayne lace strayt entree ben yates londe hongerye thenne kynge moche valyaunt man named coleman good cristen man knewe gaultier cam londe good pea tyl cam ende foude wace whiche named marce boude hongerye toward th yent passed water good pea entred ongrye witthoute knowyng gaulteer peple abode ou water cam castel named malleuylle vitaylles whiche nede hongres cause alle hoost passed sauf fewe runne vpon bette dyde ouermoche shame passed water cam gaultier shewde hym playnly ben demened without forfa ce moche grete despite moche sorowe herof passed water agayn yf grete peryl grete distourblyng thought wold goo theyr waye leue tauenge thynge long wente tyl cam belle graue whiche first cyte bongrye syde gaultier sente duc town requyred hym wolde late ther vytaylles wold suffre ony sold thoost grete disease lak vytaylle myght lenger kepe grete parte wente fowragyng gete vytaylles theyr beestys founde grete plente beestes contre whiche toke brougkt theyr lodgyngee whan contre herd armed assembled grete peple coutree ran vpon droef proyes fought toke beestes fro many slewe huted away bre wel cxl onre men shytte monasterye kepe sauf bogres cam aboute sette fyer chirche brente alle gaultier sawe ledde hym many folyssh peple whiche coude rule ne sette alle ordenauce withdrewe hym fro toke wold ruled obeye hym ffor moo thousend pylgryms whiche noman myght holde ne reteyne wold goo armed toun toun yssued many moo ayenst ther began bataylle medle grete thyk began slee eche largely peter ne route meuyd byhelde bataylle town walles wyndowes sawe theyr peple werse apperceyued grete power thoost entermeted warre thought wold helpe opened theyr yates yssued oute grete rowtes alle armed smote bataylle founde peple aboute v c vpon brygge addressyd slewe alle sauf somme caste water alle perysshed whan grete hoost apperceyued theyr peple thus euyl demened myght suffre lenger wente armes smote bataylle one aftir another lyke myght armed peple bygonne debate discomfyted fyrst began flee fast nothyng myght tarye began bete horsbak cam helpe whiche good men discomfyted cyte nygh theyr retrayt began chase moche straytly slee last whan oure peple withdrawen retorned caryage harnoys caryed alle ledde toke wymmen childeren myght flee putte prison wel slayn lost peple hoost x bongres wan alle harnoys thoost cart loste longed peter theremyte alle ful rychess whiche ben youen hym ffrauce soconre sustene necessytees hoost myght escape fro discomfiture drewe forestes hydde depe valeyes nyght morn began calle eche whystle sowne trumpes busynes woodes thus began reassemble gadred gydre territorie themperour constantynoble beyng aduertised thise oultrages sente messagers peter theremyte cao xxijo fourth daye nyghe alle assembled aboute peter four thousand moche grete meschyef lost theyr frendes theyr peple almost alle theyr harnoys withstondyng lefte wente forth waye th en erprised grete sease payne lak vytaylle poynt sawe come ayenst messagers themperour constantynoble whiche spak peter anon dyde assemble heye men capytayns hoost ere message brought aftir sayd manere ffayr syrs moche euyl tydynges renomme comen lord themperour ffor tolde hym ye goo cou tree empyre force robbe peple suche th haue breke townes slee peple doo alle oultrages wronges ye may good chere bounce alle e seruyse doon auaylleth nothyng ne may adoul e ne aswage hertes therfore commande h ye abyde none cytees thre dayes goo waye strayt forth constantynoble ffor hath commanded v goo brynge waye vytayll good cheep ynowe whan thise good men herd themperour ha boute grete ioye excused th se bataylles fyghtyng shewd openly bongres doon withoute theyr offence culpe force grete oultrag messagers dyrected way tyl cam constantynoble fonde gaultyer sans sauoyr peple taryed thene wente alle ggdre lodged place assygned eche tolde theyr mysauentures themperour sente peter wente hym sawe towne many thynges palaysses many rychesses marueylles man grete herte courage abasshyd nothyng themperour demanded hym thestate peple baron tho c yent thus meuyd pylgremage peter answerd hym moche wel alle thynges said pour peple come fore prynces hye men cam aftir moch grete peple wold long tarye themperour baron palays sawe alle peter lytil wel wysely fayr wel appoynt alle thynges answerd merueylled ouer moche alowed preysed hym moche themperour gaf hym grete yeftes receyued hym grace syth lete hym retorne peple rested oost pylgryms wel ease pea whyle aftir shippes made redy commaudement themperour passed see named braas seynt george cam lond named bythyne fyrst partye asye vpon see lodged place called cinintot mayntenyng hoost peter theremyte thre thousand duchemen toke castel assault slewe alle therin swerde capitulo xxiijo march theyr enemyes hoost two monethes euery day fonde fresshe vytaylles sell good cheep wherof wel ease moch coude wel suffred longe began meue made route goo en fourage contrey ther wente wel somtyme xm maulgre baron capytayns hoost neuetthelesse peter commanded sente lettres shold abyde remeue fro oost pylle tyl grete prynces comen daye happed pieter passed braas cam constantynoble speke vytaylles began wexe dere mene peple sawe peter hardy assembled companye wel eght thousand fote thre honderd horsback made theyr bataylles wente alle ordenauce toward cyte nycene ayenst wille deffence alle grete men thoost whan cam nyghe grete cyte smote townes toke merueyllo many beestes grete smale brought moche grete gayne retorned saufly withoute hurte home agayn oost grete ioye feste duchemen whiche ben peple rude hardy sawe glorye gayne wonne grete enuye therat meuid couetyse good haue wor hip relyed gydre alle tongue vnto nombre thre thousand foote wente strayte toward nycene castel foote hylle nygh vnto nycene leste foure myle duchemen cam theder began tassaylle castel moche strogly within defended theyr power long myght auaylled ffor castel taken force duchemen entred therin alle fonde within men wymmen chylderen slewe without mercy fode ther vytaylle ynowgh thynges sawe l ce moche fayr delectable garnysshed sayde wolde holde tyl grete prynces whome abode taryed comen solyman lord contre reprysed toke agayn castel slewe alle duchemen therin cao xxiii solyman whiche lord contre gouernoure herd longe fore cristen peple yd royamme ffraunce goo londe surye addressed passe londe therfore ben thoryent fro whens come brought grete plente knyghtes peple entended kepe londeand greue enemyes shold passe thenne drawen toward peple folkes montaynes woodes herde thys duchemen taken castel slayn men cam moost hasty wyse myghte assyeged castel toke without taryeng smote heedes alle fonde tydynge cam hoost solyman slayn alle duchemen theyr felaws moche sorow therfore ther arroos grete crye grete wepyng lodgys peple afote toke herof grete despite emonge began speke shrewdly said baron oost ought suffre shold renne horsbak auenge blood theyr bretheren nygh shed grete men thoost knewe warre thynges mene peple wold haue holden pea sayde may wel yet amended also themperour counceylled trouthe shold abyde comyng gre e baron whiche shold longe tarye peple folyssh folke content thyse wordes capytayne named godefrey bureau whiche brought suche reuerye murmur spake largely rudely ayenst knyghtes sayde alle clerly vntrewe euyl lete auenge wysedom grete cowardyse oure men armed tauenge duchemen recountour ayenst solyman cao xxvo happeth oftyme werse counseyl ouercometh better meruaylle ffor ben fooles wysemen thyse mene peple without reson meuyd moche cryed baron men hem ran armes horsbak foote wel xxv foote v c horsbak alle wel arrayed made theyr bataylles wente forth ordenaunce toward montaygnes woodes strayt toward nycene departed thre myle whan solyman whiche moche peple hym apperceyued ffor cam alle couerd secretely wode ffor make assaylle oost pylgryms whan herd noyse thaffraye foreste wyst wel thei criste men cam ayenst hym suffred passe hym self alle peple drewe hym incotinent oute wode playn shold passe whan oure peple yssued sewed sodenly toke none hede hym anon felawship ran vpon men speres swerdes tauenge theyr bretheren hethen men sawe syde certaynly wold fyghte euery man dyd beste receyued moch fiersly batayll began moche cruelle many dede bothe sydes bataylle dured longe solyman moche peple horsbacke pylgryms fote myght lenger suffre began flee without ordenaunce discomfyted turkes folowed aftir sleeyng alle myght atteyne tyl cam theyr lodgyng slayn gaultier sans sauoyr reygnald de broyes ffoucher dorleans whiche good valyaut knyghtes almost alle slayn brought prison ffor xxv men fyue honderd men horsbak coude founden thre gydre taken slayn peter theremyte beyng constantynoble aduertysed disconfyture saued thre thousand cristen men beyng grete daunger capitulo xxvio vyctorye brought solyman grete pryde grete sewr e smote lodg cristen man wer lefte thaucyet peple men wymmen clerkes monkes put alle deth fonde maydens smale childeren whiche ledde hym euer aftir seruage one side tentes nyghe vnto see old fortresse eten beten doun whiche man dwelled ne ther fonde therin dore ne wyndowe theder fledde pylgryms aboute thousand one aftir another kepe theyr lyuess ed thentrees best wyse myght grete tymbre tree grete stone turkes knewe therof cam gan tassaylle alle side moche anguysshously de ended best wey myghte ffor grete nede wh le thus assaylled messager wente h stely p ter myte constantynoble said fore message said hym alle men peryss yd sauf lytil remenaunt whiche grete meschief old hows asyeged whiche moche grete daunger yf hasty socoure peter moche abasshed meruayllously grete sorowe neuerthelesse anon ranne themperour fyld doun foot prayd hym goddes sake auacion sowle wold sende socoure poure peple grete peryll yf hasted shold alle deed themperour moche louyd peter sente anon messagers theder commanded turkes ssay ed shold leue thassault departe then wente aweye anon whan herde commandement themperour ledde prisonners yn horse mule beestes tentes pauyllons gonne wyth alle retourned nycene ye maye moche peple loste folye moyen peple whiche wold haue endure gouernaunce wyse men aboue maye men wel see grete peryl truste bataylle warre knowe preest named godechan made hym self capytayn xl duchemen viage theyr oultrages cao xxvijo syth pieter passed bythme haue said longe aftir preest named godechan prechyd duchelonde lyke peter theremyte doon ffrauce cam peple goo pylgremage ffor wel assembled xl duchemen entred alle londe hongrye ffor kyng comaunded shold receyued debonayrly cause neyghbours shold haue vytaylle necessytees pry resonable fonde londe right good began abyde alle wynter case began wexe prowd suche wyse toke away vytaylles thynges ledde awey beestes oute feeldes toke wyues bete theyr husbondes slewe noman wold leue thise oultrages kynge londe herde tydynges peple moche displaysyd moche sory therfore myght wyth honour lenger suffre lest shold torne ouermoche hurte londe subgettes dyde assemble moche peple horsbak fote tauenge thise duchemen began poursyewe ferre fonde right mydle royame c stel named bellegraue kyng seen also herd thoultrages doon londe whyles siewed aftir duchm n knewe kynge cam vpon nyghe knewe wel ben wel gouerned toward hym doon many ylle tornes wronges londe wherfor deseruyd grace loue neuirtheles ran armes sayde wolde defende fro hongers wold neuer deye nought erst wold selle theyr lyf moche dere whan kyng hongers sawe thought peple moche stronge hardy alle dispayred sawe myght ouercome without grete losse peple maner lefte force bataylle toke hym subtilite falshed peple ful barate deceyte trycherye kynge hongers sente message godechan grete men companye deceyue fayre wordes pea sayd manere ouer grete complaynte moche fowle renomme comen kyng fayr syres whiche hath sente v hether ffor hath herd saye ye haue none youre hoostes fayth ne trouthe haue taken fro hadde haue beten slayn ye haue taken doughters wyues doo suche oultrages ought sayd marcheauntes peple ye fynde wayes sure goo quyt fro robbed pyled whiche thynges kyng hath grete clamour aftir hym neuirtheles kyng knoweth wel ye alle defaulte ther ben emong many good men wyse folye moche displaysyth oultrage malefactours whiche haue angred kyng peple therfor kyng wil put defaulte one partye vpon alle ne right trewe pylgryms shold bye trespaas bad doubteth take vengeance alle wherfore couseyle ye appese kynge maner promyse good fayth ye shal neuer haue damage offre bodyes armes alle thynges wylle mercy without makyng ony appoyntement hym yf ye wil doo ye see wel ye haue puysauce ayenst hym ye myddle royamme may escape hym godechan grete men hoost oultrages moche displesyd folyes mene peple trusted wel wordes brought hade grete hope hyenes mercy kyng called peple counseyled prayde wolde rendre theyr harn y put mercy kyng wold doo sayde ther shold neuer come good put vnder vntrew peple neuertheles atte laste dyde counseyl wylle wyse men theyr harnoys alle hadde delyuerd atte commandement kynge whan supposed thereby haue goten theyr lyf ran deth ffor hongers assaylled anon mydle alle armed poynt toke none hede began slee smyte heedes without demandyng good ne euyl slewe many waded blood vnto half legge sorowe pyte see theyr bodyes fayr peple slayne stretes wayes feeldes som happed tescape wente emong retorned theyr contre tolde meschyef trayson whiche taught alle pylgryms fonde shold truste peple hongrye cc cristen men foote thre horsbak withoute capytayn assembled pylgremage theyr mayntene capitulo xxviijo litil tyme aftir grete occisyon haue said fore assembled moche grete peple foote without capytayne neuertheles ther emong hye men good knyghtes comune peple obeyed ne byleuyd nothynge emonge thomas de fere clerembault vendueyl guillem carpenter counte herman peple foote dyde many ylles oultrages waye ther arrose emong madnesse rage whiche coude kepe fro sleyng alle iewes alle wayes townes whiche passed slewe merueyllo grete nombre coleyne magonce place thise partyes wente erle right noble lord named emycon whan sawe peple put hym self theyr companye goo pylgremage chastysed ne blamed mysruled peple entysed doo euyl tornes passed francone bauyere ferre drewe hongrye cam toun naemd meeszebors wel supposed haue passed hongrye withoute ony gaynsayeng whan cam brygge deffended closed resse whiche closed one syde ryuer dunoe syde ryuernamed lintans remenaut enuyronned depe mareys within fortresse grete plente peple wel armed wherfore lyght passe toun force ffor kynge hongrye wel vnderstande comyng pe ple whiche withoute faylle wel cc fote horsbak nomoo thre thousand doubted moche whan entred londe wolde auenge tho sion doon falsehed trayson vpon peple godechan ffor rumoure speche moche yet fowle vylanous fayte thurgh al londe sawe myght passe londe prayd fortr sse wold suffre sende ssag r th kyng hongrye requyre grace myght passe good wold lodge ther whylest tho place ful pasture fore paas peple began destroye londe kyng ca se wold graunte leue passe cao xx xo lytil whyl taryed wente kyng retorned anon ffor myght spede thynges de manded kyng answerd efte ne prayer shold entre londe whan oost gre e sma e h rd moche angry ffor trauaylled desp ded moche good come thedyr loost thei wa ye concluded emong hey shold brenne destro ye contreye kynge moche syde mareys sette fyer townes toke men de troyed alle contrey whyles dyde thus peple fortre cam peple kyn g nombre knyghtes peple wel armed passed shippes er euer pligrims knewe ony w sette f r deffende pylgryms paas shold entre whan pylgryms sawe ran vygorously vpon suche wyse er myght saue self slayn alle sauf fewe withdrewe mareys ydde whan thyse p lgryms thus vict ye ey mounted moche grete hardynes said force wold take fortresse hongrye withoute leue wold passe thurgh londe thenne began somonne recomforte euery man doo wel toke pole made scaffholdes moche grete plente whiche sette walles mounted vp couerd theyr sheldes targes assaylled moche hardely many pyked pykoys myned walles grete force thentre semed al redy entree within nyghe deed despayer ffor defended slowly men affrayed hertes ffor supposed anon slayn sodenly cam fere drede vpon hertes pylgryms wened anon slayn neuer knowen wherfore anon fyl donn fro scaffoldes taryed fledde sodeynly none wyste fledde hongers whan sawe myght wyth grete peyne byleue trouthe ffor sawe rayson neuertheles whan apperceyuyd descended doun began folowe chaas suche wyse next fore almost alle taken slayn auenture fonden none reson sauf peple ful synne deseruyd loue lord ne thonoure world therfor theyre synnes acowarded suche wyse myght doo ne accomplysshe grete werke whiche nyghe achyeued erle emycon cam agayn contre grete nombre peple disconfyted baron ffraunce fore haue named wente lombardye puylle knowleche grete baron passed dura fro then grece wente aftir folowyd manere peple ffraunce disperpled contrees ther waye hongrye moche strayte ner yf myght haue goon destrowbled theyr folye cam aftir peyned moche goo wysely pea duc godefroy boloyne beyng grete hoost cam vnto hongrye sente messagers kyng demande passage capitulo xxxo comen moneth anguste yere thyncarnacion lord lxxxxvj xv day moneth valyaut godefroy buyllon duc loraygne assembled shold felawes iourneye cam fro contrey grete apparayllement apperteyned estate hym bawdwyn brother bawdwyn erle henawde huge erle seynt pol euerard sone moche valyaunt yonge man garnyer erle surnamed grees bernard erle toul pieter brother bauwdwyn de bors cosyn duc henry dasque godefr brother many good knyghtes thise men good frendes emonge wyse men wyse wold departe one fro cam alle hool thynges osteryche xx daye septembre vnto town named taylleborch reneth ryuer named yntans departed thempyre allemaygne fro royamme hongrye whan comen theder herd waye euyl dynges grete mesauentures godechan peple hongrye assembled toke counseyl emonge myght passe contre pea alle acorded shold sende messagers lettres vnto kyng hogrye demande first reason theyr felaws pylgryms whic e theyr bretheren thus perysshed power londe aftir encharged messagers shold ntre hym coicacion myg passe ro seurly pea herin put deu payne ffor waye moche shorte couenable yf myght haue pas message wente godefroy da ue brother henry cause long fore ben acqueynted kynge hongrye ith sente wyse men wente fo f r fonde kyn salewed hym name hem sen e th delyuerd lettres credence aftir sayd hym thyse wordes messagers duc godefroy declared message vnto kyng hongrye ther vpon answere cao xxxio wyse man noble godefroy duc yne prynces hym come pylgremage aue sente v vnto wolde knowe occasion pylgryms helde felaw bretheren haue cruelly slayn smeton piece wer wel knowe sende worde haue ben slayn ffor haue fonden many ben escaped moche meruaylle ye peple ben cristen ye saye haue thus destroyed good companye whiche enhause fayth ihesu crist ben departed theyr contre suche wyse mortal enemyes haue werse desire moche knowe yf defaulte pylgryms ffor yf ye haue doon iustyce deffendyng youre londes wyse wold enforce take ony thyng away yf duc felaws wold take lightly yf doo without trespaas hate ye thus murdred sente v hether lete wete v haue lefte theyr owne coutreyes tauenge wronges oultrages haue ben peple oure lord yf finde ye haue doo wylle passe ferther tyl haue theyr power auenged deth pylgryms lord herwith godefroy acounted kyng made ende wordes kyng palays grete plente baron royamme peple thenne answerd sayde godefroy plesyth moche ye come contrey speke moche good thyng two cause one ye myn acqueyntauce frende longe syth shal afferme renewe loues acqueyntaunces youre comyng cause knowe man wyse resonable good wille moche ioyous ye shal excusacion trouthe haue name cristiente shold moche fayr v yf werkes ben passed tofore peter theremyte godechan haue werkes pylgryms ne cristen men ffor receyuyd peter theremyte peple oure londes townes grete debonayrte departed oure vytaylles thynges gaf lyke serpent prycketh styngeth hym kepeth hym warme bosomme hath guerdonned rewarded v good dedes thende royamme hongrye whan ought thanke v rendre grace god theyr frendes toke force one oure best castellis put deth alle therin caryed beestys toke alle maydens town lyke rowters theues company godechan cam abode forfaytte til ende royamme assone entred passed yates hongrye began make alle thoultrages myghte brente townes slewe men enforced wymmen bare away alle thynges dyde moche theyr trespaces wel worthy haue hate god world place dygnyte whiche ought kepe peple long shal please god baron haue sworn feaulte royalme myght wel endure thus destroye peple contrey haue put hand force v defendyng thyrde companye cam also folke foote doubted noyse debate suche wyse wold suffre entre londe ne come emonge v lord iugeth alle wordes knoweth alle thyng wote wel thus haue lyed worde praye ye excuse v oueraal ye shal speke whan said sente messagers theyr innes moche grete honour grete feste kyng toke counseyl baron ordeyned owne messagers whiche sente duc godefroy prynces cam spoken ynowgh godefroy dasque made hym grete c ere gaf hym felawshippe yeftes aftir toke leue hym retorned al gydre messagers whan comen fore duc godefroy one sayd message manere kyng hongrye saleweth lordes sendeth yow worde knoweth certaynly renome ye man moche hye lygnage puyssaut peple wyse trewe herte prudent valyaunt body suche wyse prouesse born many londes ffor thyse thynges lord kynge whiche neuer sawe yow preyseth loueth yow moche herte hath moche grete desire doo honoure pylgryme ben haue enterprysed hye pylgremage preyseth moche desyreth moche see worshippe haue theyr acqueyntaunce ffor holdeth hym selfe wrous gracious lord hath sette hym poynt may doo seruyse bounte one valyaunt man therfore vnto fayr lord hye men companye prayeth requyreth demandeth synguler yefte wold plese come see hym one castel named cipe ffor desireth moche speke leyser doo ye wille demaude said kynge sente fetche duc godefroye wente deuyses gydr cao xxxij whan duc baron herd messager thus speke drewe parte toke counseyl acorded wel duc shold goo sente suche companye h wold haue wente forth thre honderd horse withoute way hit long cam aperon passed brygge fonde kynge whiche made hym grete ioye moche honour long spak gydre kynge excused hym deth pylgryms vnto duc lyke doon messagers thende kyng cam poynt appeased goodly kyng acorded hym passage thurgh royamme yf wold sette hym suche hoostages shold chese kepe pee alle graunted demanded hostage bawdwyn brother sayd duc wyf maygne delyuerd hym gladly thus entred alle theyr peple lond hongrye kynge helde wel couenauntes ffor dyde doo crye alle townes shold passe also thereby shold selle vytaylles good cheep noman shold meue debate duc commanded also made cryed none payne lyf hardy take ony thynge fro lond ne fro man ne doo wronge holde felawes bretheren thus happed passed alle hongrye without ony maner stryf noyse kynge rode alwey nyghe thooste lyfte syde ledyng hostage hym redy tappese yf ony noyse arroos atte laste cam malleuylle wherof ye haue herd fore whiche stondeth ryuer dunoc tyl alle hoost passed shippes wherof fewe fore sette ouer thousand men wel armed kepe arryuyng syde whan hoos comyn peple passed kyng cam duc baron brought hostage delyuerd hym made moche ioye honour departyng gaf euerych grete yiftes ryche aftir toke leue retorned home ageyn duc baron passed ouer peple cam bellegraue cyte hongrye whiche haue spoken fore lodged passed thurgh wodes til cam cyte nyz stralyce duc godeffroye sente messagers themperour constantinoble thende shold delyuer huon le mayne helde prison capo xxxiijo may knowen euyl disposicion deceyte grekes ffor syth themperours latyns faylled constantynople thempyre cam vnto grekes fyrst nycofores anon barbaryns aboute blacz comans hongrye whiche ben toward eest supprised toke thyse londes good plentyuous delytable conquerd alle fro dunoe vnto constantinople parte vnto see adryane cyte lombardye nygh londe marquys named adre right litil cyte cause nygh see venyse ancone hath see name see adryane wrytyng see goth right nygh constantinoble vnto xxx myle euyl peple thempyre constantinoble wel wonue vpon grekes xxx iourneyes lengthe x brede ffor aboue see haue spoken countre named epyre chyef cyte named dura whiche pycrus somtyme kynge another named mayene myddle londe ben also noble cytees nyz stralyce londe archade thessale machedone thyse thre landes euerych called trace alle thise conquerd vpon grekes afterward ther emperour named basilie recouerd thise londes brought blacz bongres longe afore tyme suche wyse two danemarches comen agayn po wer yet wold grekes suffre repayre agayn townes ne laboure lode shold right good thende none shold enhabyte cause holde strengthe nothyng shold fonde therin also espyre whiche extendeth fro dura vnto mount named bagula endureth foure iourneyes passed baron duc companye passed danemarche la en whiche named wyse mese cam destrayte whiche named cloys e seynt basyle syth descended playne fonde grete plente vytaylle pasture cam vnto ine po whiche moche fayr cyte good herd saye trouthe themperour constantynoble enprisonned huon le mayne broder kynge ffraunce many baron cam hym ffor thise noble men hasty cam lombardye puylle ffro then passed dura soiourned tabyde baron whiche ought come tho partyes ne supposed haue doubted ony thyng londe grekes cristen baylly dura toke alle moost grete baron sente yrons themperour constantynoble doo wylle helde prison abode comyng baron cause yf cam grete power wolde delyuer theyr loue yf cam grete myght thought lyghtly lete passe whan duc godefroye baron herd tydynges delyuere retourned hoost said thansuer themperour whan duc baron herd moche wroth concluded emong theyr counseyl wold playnly make warre ayenst hym dyde grete oultrage holde hye prynce prison ne wolde answere mesure ne reason habandonned hooste take contre alle coude fynde brente alle townes thus abode thise partyes destroyed alle contre dyde moche grete dommage harme grete plente proyes gaynes cam constantynoble tassiege toun anon yssued oute huon mayne doene dancelle guylla ne charpentier clarembault de venduel entred auyllon duc thanked hym moche alle theyr delyueraunce duc hooste receyued moche grete ioye ffor moche grete ang e gre despite grete despyte themperour toke duc godeffroy reffused goo constatinoble vnto hym capo xxxv whyles spak thus gydre cam messagers fro themperour duc requyred theyr lordes name wold entre fewe companye town come speke themperour duc counseyl herupon answerd wold yet come toune whan themperour herd therof moche grete despite deffended oueral ther shold nomore v taylle sold ne none thynges noble men sawe sente fouragyng ouer alle countrey brought vytaylle grete plente suche wyse ynowgh poure ryche themperour sawe contre shold destroyed doubted kepte sawe alle cyte meued armed come men thenne adcerteyned towne theyr enemyes sette fyer howses lodged whiche doubted fered wel vj thousand seuen suche wyse som emperours owne howses brente dyde swollen angry lost many men ben euyl demened began ordeyne thurgh town myght yssue oute moche affraye strenger nyght cam destourned counseyl euident thynge themperour n baron passe brygge tricherye vntrouthe haue closed within barryers peple began destroye contre ofa message buymont vnto duc godefroye answer duc vpon capitulo xxxviijo sone thoost apperceyued morn day cryed euery man payne deth shold arme hym horsbak fote capytayns som bataylle ordeyned lede peple fourage sette ordynaunce kepe lodgys ffor wel apperceyued certaynly themperour pourchassed alle euyl myght wente vytaylle withdrewe wel lx myle pylled al aboute alle townes fonde brought corn wyn beestys rychesses wherof londe full vnnethe myght conduyte alle oute sex dayes aftir retornned hooste alle merueillous gayne whyles conteyned thus messagers cam fro buymont fore duc salewed hym theyr lordes name delyuerd hym lettres whiche saide manere salewed letrres duc ought salewe suche man aftir sayde knowe ye sire ye haue doo moche vntrewe man whiche alwey sette herte purpoos deceyue truste hym specially hateth latyns deth doth power alle maners doo euyl peple yf ye haue yet apperceyued ye shal knowe al tyme saye ffor knowe wel malyce grekes also trycherye themperour therfor pray ye withdrawe fro constantinoble retorne ward playnes andrenoble sympole ye may wyntre grete plente alle goodes self yf please god assone sprynge yere cometh shal come hast meue shal assemble shal helpe lord frende ayenst vntrew prynce entendeth doo euyll alle power vnto cristiente whan duc herd thyse lettres couseyl baron sente hym ageyn lettres salewyng spak thus thanke gretely doo prynces ben v loue trouthe ye haue sente v knowe ye certaynly haue founden prynce peple grekes lyke ye wene wel knowe knowe wel ye saye wysedome constantynople fore themperour moche desyred grekes made grete ioye merueyllously someuer thoughte themperour kyssed alle demanded euerych name honoure euerych hym self wel coude wel beholden alle palays last themperour satte mageste baron aboute hym sayde duc thyse wordes haue herd saye many tymes londe thou art hyghe lygnage moche grete power thy contre good knyght trewe suche wyse fayth ihesu criste enhaunce hast enterprised warre ayenst mescreauntes hethen peple whiche greue cristen peple merueyllously ffor alle thyse thynges prayse loue herte wylle honoure grettest honour may doo ffor thou art worthy dygne playseth v therto acorden baron cheese auowe sone put empyre thyn hande thou kepe sone henssforth good estate termes loue whan seyde dyde hym clad robe emperour sytte hym thenne baron made hym right grete feste solempnyte aftir custom londe suche thynges thus pee affermed bytwene prynces also bytwene peple yeftes themperour made duc godefroye baron gentilmen weke moche two myghty men myght susteyne pierrye pen gold copper tyn gaf hym ten muyes euery muye four busshellys duc departed alle thyse thynges vnto knyghtes alle aboute sawe shold wel employed whan herte preyse praye moche acertaynly requyre grete yefte thou doo thy peple passe contrees without oultrages doyng harme haste come v alle sure haue oure grace oure bounte haue comanded vytaylles necessy ee shal sold thy peple pry resonable whan erle alle baron herde thise tydynges thyse lettres glad ioyous ffor longe suffred grete disease toke theyr waye forestes montaynes passed londe epyre aftir cam pelagonne fonde moche grete plente alle goodes valyaunt bisshop puy lodged hym day fer fro hoost fayr place founde nyght bongres assaylled hym lodgys toke hym cause necessarye cristiente hym requyred hym right swetly haue alwey alyaunce amytre hym also grete prouffyt shold haue therof shold make hommage themperour lyke alle answerd shortly wold none make ne doo hym themperour grete themperour comaunde surely cause wyste wel othersyde myght helpe cause men wold ne greue commaunded alle shippes bere ouer vytaylle sholde come hastely ageyn cyte syde shold come ouer gayn ffor euer suspection thassemble oure peple therfore made passe ouer eche cam grete chere made grete yeftes gaf cam barate drede loue largesse oure peple specially ffrenssmen myght byleue ioye made ne rychesse gaf myght come ony trayson ne euyl knewe experyence moche thene dyde afterward themperour tauenge hym therle made conestables tenbusshe assaylle hoost therle ca xlviijo conestables whiche commandement themperour spak gydre theyr men made bus ement nyghe hooste erle tholouse nyght whan supposed alle well assured themperours peple smote emong slewe wounded many awaked apperceyued whan crye arroos noble men thooste apperceyued trayson armed reteyned theyr peple began flee ran vpon themperour slewe many chassed remenaunt morn hooste began moche esmayed trauaylle suffred nyght trayson grekes theyr hertes began cole faylle purpoose theyr waye pylgremage smal comune peple many grete noble men forgoten theyr vowes theyr honour wold haue retorned home vnto theyr countrey noble bisshop puy bi op orenge emonge many good wyse relygyous men clerkys prechyd wordes lord recomforted moche wel shewde yf retourned shold lese thonour world also thus grete peyne reteyned whan erle whiche constantynople herde trayson hym hoost man wytte anon sente men themperour sente hym word betrayde hym ffor whyles reteyned hym made hym good chere doo slee peple trayson sente worde herof baron syde prayeng bretheren wold come hym auege wel may ye knowe yf therle power sufficient wold haue departed tyl auengyd hym shold haue ben dere bought ffor man grete courage forgate lyghtly shame hym themperour sawe thynge goon ouer ferre suche wyse repented hym commaunded angre hastynes hasted hym moche sette counseyl werke sente buymont therle fflaundres come speke hym cause wold sende appese therle tholouse cam whiche moche angry wente therle name themperour sayd hym theyr owne behalue themperours shewde hym wel tyme ne place tauenge shame ben hym seruyse oure lord ffor shold empesshement whiche deyde waye houndes chace huntyng fowles flyght ffawcons hawkes fperhawkes ye shold haue seen day abyde deye lyke wyse grete stedes cursours whiche moost peryllo becam alle araged wood thurst grete payne ledde forth whan ben long mesease lord beheld pyte made adresse valeye fonde rennyng water fayr grete thene ranne oure peple brynke ryuage grete haste many ther drak moch deyde vpon place ffor som eschewed deth fonde cause kepte mesure fylle vnto knyghtes men beestes whiche dranke moche wolde whan escaped euyl aduenture cam londe moch fayr fertile ful woodes ryuers medowes good feldes labourable anthyoche lasse whiche chyef cyte londe pisside lodged theyr hoost somme grete baron thoost haue approuched antyoche lasse departed goo vytaylle capitulo lxviijo fro then departed som baron thoost elde waye cause greuous thyng fynde vytaylles moche peple gydre fyrst bawdwyn brother duc hym peter therle scaruay reynart therle oul bawdwyn de borgh guyllebert de montcler ther wer wel vc horsbak ladde men fote largely second tancre hym rychard du pryncipat robert danse knyghtes grete nombre v c horsbak also many men foote theyr entecion purpose ride thoost contre seche somme aduenture vytaylle yf founde ony paryll grief pa plente theyr enemyes wold ete thoost haue knowleche therof wente strayt theyr waye passed syde ij cytees one named lychonie eraclee th torned right honde passed toward see side duc godeffroy prynces abode theyr lodgys plesaunt delytable place fouden cause wolde playe refresshe trauaylles anoyes suffred thenne said wold goo hunte forestes nygh alle sydes ful wilde beestes morn entred woode eche helde way duc wente path thurgh foreste herde man crye drewe thederward sawe poure man goo fetche wode bere hoost fledde strongly cryeng fore grete bere duc ran vpon hym drewe swerd delyuere pour man fro beeste thenne bere adressyd hym vnto duc lefte pour man fledde fro hym hurte duke hors sore caste duc therthe duc foote drewe oute swerde beeste nothyng af rd hym made felonno crye horryble hydous syth ran vpon duc bote hym right cruelly thye adressyd hym right vp embraced hym po e foot fore haue caste hym groude duc thus hurt yet moch strog fyl theerthe thene caught hym skyn reck lyfte hande put away heed hym hand put swerd body thurgh bothe sydes vnto crosse slewe hym wente sette hym doun therthe right ffor moche bledde wounde thy merueyllously sore hurte myghte stonde longe foot poure man whiche delyuerd fro deth hastely hoost tolde tydynge duc alle herde effrayed ranne grete haste theder baron alle myght goo founde hym lyeng ground pale discoloured toke hym lyttier bare hym hoost neuer man demened ne sorow made r noe moo pytyous cryes lamentacions thurgh alle lodgyses wel ryche poure men wymmen anon fette alle maistres cirurgens dychte hym hele hym many ffor euerych prynces awayte hoost recounteth thystorye somme aduentures thenne fylle hoost cristen men capo lxixo sayson tyme happed another valyaut man named raymont erle tholouse laye doun seke maladye moche greuous peryllous neuerthel sse hoost wente forth alwey therfor muste caryed forth lytt er day happed deteyned maledye certeynly supposed shold deye kep e hym made littier sette doun grounde ffor sawe hym feble thought certaynly sowle shold departe bisshop orenge whiche moche holy man reli gyous sayd commendacion sowle seruyse one deyeng sauf syngyng masse alle hoost ouermoche discomforted cause supposed alle anon sodanly lese thise two grete men whiche moche gre e counseyl grete ayde made prayer orysons thurgh alle thoos songe mass ryche pour prayde moche humbly good herte lord wold rendre hool sauf oure counseyle nede baron departed charyte largely alm sse vnto pour peple moche dyde one oure lord whiche ful pyte herde gaf helthe two noble men short tyme suche wyse rood al hool good poynt thooste passed al pissyde entred lande named lycaone cam vnto cyte called founde alle voyde nothyng therin grete meseases vytaylle ffor turkes whiche herde tydynges oure peple cam trusted none theyr fortress voyded fledde forestes montaynes men wymmen childeren horse eestes vytaylle alle thyng caryed suffred moche disease passe contre cam eracle cam cyte named marase lodged soiourned thre dayes bawdwyn brother duc departed fro hoost lefte wyf two br theren deyde sekenesse hye lady englond valyant wyse good gutier name buryed entrered moche honorably place moche waylled hoost tancre departed fro hoost assieged tarse toke certeyn couenaunt capo lxxo tancre whiche wyse man grete courage rode thurgh londe sekyng auenture suche wyse fonde waye cyte called tarse londe scylyce cou tre theryent toward sonne gooyng doun lande ben two grete cytees whiche ben archebisshoprichs one named tarse whiche said fore therin born seynt poul thappostle named anauazie eche thise two cytees haue cytees vnder tarse founded one childeren noe ionen whiche sone iaphet sone noe neuerthles souns sayth perseus founded maye wel one founded repayred amended tancre assieged cyte constreyned within menace fayr wordes yelded hym manere sette banere vpon hyest toure toun swar affermed kepe damage hurte ne non shold put hows ne lese ony thyng apperteyned vnto comynge grete hoost thenne shold yelde toun vnto grete prynces thoost without ony debate thus acorded bytwene hym toun toun cristen men hermyns grekes alle londe turke helde alle fortress medled armes seygnorye vpon peple wold suffre nothyng sauf occupye laboure therthe marchaunte bye selle bawdwyn brother godeffroy sechyng auentures sawe tacre peple fore tarse adressed hym ca lxxj bawdwyn brother duc peple ledd hym entred countre moost barayn suffred grete peyne vytaylle cam vpon montayne myght see alle londe scilice cytees vnto see sawe tarse nygh pauyllons supposed turkes assieged cyte descended doun knowe peple also tenquere beyng countre tancre thauaunt garde sawe thyse men armes approuche lete theyr lord haue knowleche tancre wende certaynly turkes cam socoure toun made eche man arme hym dylygently sette ordenaunce yssued oute ayenst baners displayed whan approuched one knewe eche armes opened theyr helmes embraced eche made moche grete ioye cam cyte thenne bawdwyn tancre right wel honourably lodged ffor tancre grete plente vytaylles whiche bawdwyn peple grete nede thenuye bawdwyn peple see baner tancre vpon walle toun tancre departed ca lxxijo morne whan sonne vp cleer daye bawdwyn hym sawe baner tancre vpon hyest tour toun therof moche grete enuye began murmure speke maliciously gretter power moo peple better said ought haue worship toun trouthe vnto day bawdwyn tancre ben lyke two bretheren moche pryue acqueyntaunce trewe loue bawdwyn enuye herte euyl wordes som men made hym vnderstonde thus thynge meuyd tancre whiche moche wyse attemperat resonable man vnderstode thise wrodes dyde moche payne tapesse hym cam persone bawdwyn shewde hym fore comen ne noman knewe comynge thyse couenauntes made bytwene hym toune baner sette vpon toure herin vnderstode myght haue ony shame ne dishonour baudwyn content thise wordes founde somme attysed hym folye spak grete wordes ylle iniuryouses tancre suche wyse lytil wolde haue armed theyr men haue destroyed eche thene sente bawdwyn toun whan cam menaced strongly saide shold throwe doun baner tancre therthe sette vp tour yf dyde shold wel knowe wold destroye alle without toun take toun caste therthe maulgre alle tancre myght doo cyte sawe tancre myght waraunte ne deffende ayenst bawdwyn made hym suche couenauntes made fore tancre sette baner commaunded tancre saw force hym gretely displesyd grete yre herte couerd thought wysely wold suffre peple comen pylgremage make warre ayenst thenemyes fayth ihesu crist shold slee eche thoccasion hym departed fro place ffor doubted somme noyse medle myght sourde herof cam cyte nygh named adane myght entre ffor noble man burgoyn named gelphes parted fro thoost grete route men armes dyde seke auentures taken cyte force caste turkes helde entierly tancre herde somme peple helde sente good messagers gelphes prayd hym opene yates suffre men myght goo toun bye suche neded gelphes dyde debonayrly hym self gaf largely nought ffor founde toun ful gold syluer robe beestes whete wyne oyle alle good man nede lytil tancre cam cyte anamystre whiche turkes helde toke assault capo lxxiijo tancre morn toke leue hooste toke way peple rode fer cam cyte named anamystre one beste cytees londe fayr moche delytable tancre cam theder knewe certeynly turkes helde assieged al aboute fro tyme cam assaylled toun thus dyde first second thirde day many assaultes made hurted toun strongly greuyd abasshed without toke toun entred vnder walles thus toun taken force alle fonde therin hethen peple put deth without mercy toune ful rychesses alle maner vytaylles grete plente tancre departed al gayn goodes toun men wel knewe shold doo eche man suche wyse alle men ryche refresshed moche wel theyr beestes mesease suffred theyr waye soiourned grete whyle moche grete deduyt bawdwyn entred tarse iijc pylgryms slayn turkes fore toun ca olxxiiij baudwyn sawe tancre departed fro tarse sente toun sayde shold lete entre toun ffor hym thought shame lye long abyde ydle without doyng ony thyng tyl comynge grete hoost sawe aduysed wel power ynough resiste thought yf lete entre theyr agreement wold entre ayenst theyr wylle without force thene opened gate wold bawdwyn shold haue two toures shold lodge thoste howses toun alle peasibly turkes seygnorye toun helde yet towres theyr puissaunce moche grete doubte suspection bawdwyn men lodged toun thought shold haue socours aboue moche grete drede grete hoost shortly shold arryue sought emonge moyens maner myght yssue oute toun lede theyr wyues childeren theyr pryncipal bageus iewellys happed nyght thre honderd men afore departed fro buymont folowe tancre arryued alle fore cyte tarse thought fynde hym whan bawdwyn knewe peple wente thayde tancre wold suffre entre toun wery trauaylled prayd hym moche swetly cryed hym mercy many tymes loue god wold doo moche myght nyght lodged toun ffor wold nothyng good herof fotemen companye prayd hym lyke wise wold nowyse neuertheles cause without mesease mene peple toun aualed doun cordes breed ynough wyn barellys vytaylles whiche myght wel passe nyght whan peple slepe toun without began theyr first sleep happed turkes within toures opened yates whiche keyes secretely withoute noyse ledde wyues theyr childeren alle thynges alle hethen men toun thought sure theyr ghestes yssued alle toun whan theyr wyues childeren withdrawen lytil fro toun wolde leue tokenes cruell ylle theyr departyng cam vnto thre honderd pylgrims laye withoute gate slepte strongly doubted nothyng put alle deth slewe yf ony escaped happy peple bawdwyn knewe departyng turkes slaughter cristen men capo lxxvo morne erly whan oure men awoke toun sawe toures turkes lodged open howses voyde knewe wel fledde serched walles yates enquyre goon wente ferre fonde grete occis slaughter gate thenne began sorow moche grete crye toun alle men put blame culpe bawdwyn hys knygtes ffor wold auenge deth theyr bretheren sarasyns shamely vylaynously slayn cause knyghtes bawdwyn also hym self wold suffre come toun dede men foote sayd grete oultrage grete falshede yf lyghtly withdrawen toures smyten alle deth knyghtes helde alle stylle tyl footemen cooled sente messagers whiche spak requyre forbere long tyl bawdwyn spoken content bawdwyn speke bawdwyn excused hym fore e swar affermed none thynge thentre deffended sworn toun hym shold none entre tyl grete hooste cam thyse wordes cause entermeted make pea spoken debonayrly mene peple bawdwyn acorded foote man knyghtes also toun soiourned abode certayn whyle vntyl mornyng sawe see nygh shippe aboute myle fro yssued oute toun descended see ship approched wyse spak gydre ship sayde cristen men demaunded contre answerd fflaundres holande ffryselande trouth escumours see robber space viij yere repented penaunce cam pylgremage iherusalem desyred come londe cam made gydre grete ioye maister ouer named guynemer born boloyne vpon see londe erle eustace fader said duc godeffroy whan e herde bawdwyn sone lord e lefte ship said wold goo hym iherusalem moche ryche euyl gayne many men hym ladde ship thenne bawdwyn lefte v c men armes kepe toun wel poynt toke waye seke somme auentures dyde fore e helde right way al cam cyte anamyster whiche tancre goten force armes vpon turkes haue sayd fore bawdwyn thought wel wold lete hym entre cyte therfor lodged hym th gardyns tancre knowe bawdwyn whiche loued hym nygh hym e forgoten wronge oultrage bawdwyn hym thenne dyde arme men sayde thenne tyme venge hym ffor nygh retrayt bawdwyn fro sente archiers fore grete nombre hurte slee theyr horse whiche sente pasture tancre hym fyue honderd men armes good poynt wel horsed smote sodanly peple bawdwyn whiche aduysed slewe many moo hurted men bawdwyn ran hastely arme cam fought ran tentes ther began bataylle bytwene moche grete fiers ndured nge ffor tancre grete plente peple myght endure ayenst n bawdwyn therfor wold withdrawe theyr toun theyr enemyes enchassed strongly moche muste flee brygge ouer water bytwene hooste cyte peple tancre entred thyck many lost slayn vpon brygge drowned water whan put toune agayn moche angry theyr herte wold take peple returne agayn nyght cam destroubbed scarmuche taken rychard le pryncipat cosyn germayn tancre robert danse two noble men counseyl atysement tancre ronne vpon bawdwyn syde taken moche noble man named gylbert de mountcler moche angry one syde loste ffor doubted ben slayn drowned whan cam morn theyr hertes lytil aswaged sente messagers eche knewe certaynly thyse men taken lyued dredde ben deed good men wente byt wene medled speke pee suche wyse cam agayn entier concordaunce parfyght loue grace holy ghoost adressyd theyr hertes amended theyr trespaas eche kyssed gydre frendes good fayth sayd bawdwyn retorned grete hooste tancre mayntenyd hym moche wel conqueryng contrees capitulo lxxvjo bawdwyn counseyl whan come maraze haue recompted shold goo ferther forth retorned thoos baron cause herd saye duc brother hurte peryllously wold see knowe estate ferde theyr counseyl tancre shold goo forth bawdwyn lefte hym guy neuers companye comen fro shippe passed alle syly e bete doun alle forestes hethen men myght fynde brente townes slewe theyr enemyes cam vnto cyte called alexandrye lasse toke force conquerd al c ntre hermyns turkes dwellyd montaynes contre herde tydynges tancre men valyaunt myghty nothyng myght holde ayens sore dredde lyke conquerd playne wold come vpon montaynes destroye londe entierly peple ffor tappease courage sente ta hym good certeyn messagers whiche brought hym grete yeftes gold syluer precious stone clothes sylk horse mubett sente hym moche largely ffor whiche cause tancre lefte pea thus dyde wel honoure pronffyt alle place went suche wyse semed wel euery man oure lord god adressyd way mayntened w rkes vertuosly bawdwyn conquerd grete contre vpon turkes counseyl knyght bermyn named panc ace cao lxxvijo ye haue herd tancre nayntened hym sylyce grete hoost folowed hym cam vnto marase bawdwyn seen brother duc hool sound herd agayne tydynges tancre dyde contre wente e moch grete desire gadre gydre peple goo serche cotre lyke dyde fore lost moche good wyl grace thoost ffor thoost herd tolde thoultrage e tancre men therfore many doub ed entreprise way hym buymont men also lyghtly suffred thyng vn auengyd ne ad ben loue duc brother therfor bawdwyn founde ewe felawes wold goo hym godeffroy duc moc e wyseman good wyll blamed rep e yd moche brother werke brought hym herto e knowleched folye fore alle peple sayde made amedes tancre yet wolde amende vnto playsyr swar doon counseyl aty ement hym self thyse wordes e appeasyd hertes many men ffor moche valyaunt man moch curt y neuer per yued hym vylo e myne hym moche pryue named pan ra e right wyse hardy knyght ouermoche trycherous vntrewe escaped oute prison themperour constantynoble cam hoost nycene acqueynted hym bawdwyn prayd hym admonested shold take men goo countre shold lede hym whiche moche plentyuous ful goodes yf wold goo shold conquere lightly ofte said hym herof began take way departed two honderd knyghtes men armes ynough feotemen grete nombre folowed pancrace alle whiche brought ward byse moch ryche lond dwellyd londe alle cristen men sauf fewe turkes whiche helde fortress lordes contre suffred cristen men shold meddle ony armes wyse whan oure fayth sawe bawdwyn men glad ioyeful ffor loued turkes delyuerd ouer contre puyssaunce suche wyse short tyme conquerd alle londe vnto flood eufrates bawwyn moch drad doubted thurgh alle contre ther wyse drede lefte hym alle fortress wel garnysshed toke without debate cristen men whiche receyued hym londe bycam fiers hardy hunted alle hethen men contre ther somme baron contre seruyd bawdwyn alle theyr puyssaunce heelpe hym brynge alle thyng wylle rage sente theyr messagers bawdwyn prayeng hym wold come capo lxxviijo renome grete man prowesse wytte spredde oueral cam vnto cytezeyns rage hopyng hym delyuerid seruage whiche ben long grettest men gouernaunce toun sente certayn messagers bawdwyn prayd hym loue god honoure prouffyt wold come vnto theyr cyte whiche named rage founden byble thether sente thobye sone yong thobye demaunde moneye gable cosyn ought hym way wedded sara wyf cytezeyns cyte receyued cristen fayth anon deth oure lord ihesu criste prechyng seynt iude appostle brother seynt symon foude wre book eusebee ce aire helde yet fermly lawe tyme turkes constreyned moch made paye greuous grete tribute euery yere moche whan tyme cam gadre theyr fruytes theyr vynes raunsouned muste paye theyr wylle ellys wolde destroye alle neuertheles toun durst noman dwelle byleuyd ihesu criste ffor toun holden hool entierly fayth hethen peple conquerd townes therfor greued moche cristen peple toun ne wold suffre yssue toun doo theyr nedes ffor alle sydes puyssaunce turkes toun seygnorye greek moche oold childeren ben syth tyme londe vnder themperour constantynoble ffor sente thyder themperour fro baylly whan turkes toke alle countrey departed then abode alwey baylliage neuertheles e made neyther hoot ne cold ne kept peple theyr wyll whan cytezeyns acorded sende bawdwyn knewe wel content whan bawdwyn herde rage sente hym comyn couseyl corde toke couseyl men fonde counseyl goo theder ordeyned lxxx horsme without moo goo hym passed ryuer eufrates lefte remenaunt peple fortress coquerd cotre kepe surely turkes dwellyd lade knewe tydynges bawdwyn shold come rage fewe men made embusshement waye shold passe sette grete plente men armes thyse tydynges wer sayde bawdwyn therfor torned castel whiche hermyn helde receyued hym gladly al men moch honorably lodged ij dayes turkes en oyed long embusshed yssued cam baners displayed fore castel bawdwyn inne none yssued ther ouer many men proye founde pa ures brought alle torned theyr countrey thirde daye bawdwyn yssued toke waye cam rage duc toun greek haue said fore cam ayenst hym alle horsbak foote trompes busyn e peple toun receyued hym procession moost honorably myght euerych peyned hym make hym feste puyssaunce duc rage varyed holde promysed bawdwyn capitulo lxxixo grete suspection duc herte whan sawe ioye alle made bawdwyn thenne enuye began fynde occasion whiche myght parte fro couenau te suche sente whiche suche bawdwyn shold haue half rente alle cyte alle thexploytes long duc lyued deth whiche olde shold haue alle seygnorye entierly hool duc wold holde sayde yf bawdwyn wold deffende cyte fro strengthe turkes fro theyr gryeues made countre wold gyue hym men resonable souldye good wage whan bawdwyn herd come theder souldyour moche grete desdayne sayd wold abyde wold ordeyn hym men retorne cytezeyns toun sawe thyng wente wel cam duc shewde hym grete euyl peryll shold folowe yf lete noble departe ffor thayde hym alle theyr thynges shold kept pea deffended shold grete franchys duc sawe wel thyse wordes shold folye yf sette hym ayenst toun therfore couerd herte tyme withstondyng considered many thynges thought sayde wold acorde therto made semblaunt dyde good wille presence alle toun auowed bawdwyn sone graunted hym half alle shold haue lyf duryng decees haue alle heyr grete ioye cyte whan made moost ferme hope recounte franchyse trubutes turkes charged ffro day forth began remembre theyr hertes wronges gryefs theyr duc tyme passed thought moche yf tyme place cam poynt wold suffre lenger thought myght auenge suffred alle tyme duc bawdwyn wente assaylle famosette cyte nyghe rage capitulo lxxxo cyte nyghe moche stronge wel garnysshed named famosette vntrew turke named blanduc lord therof trychour noble hardy armes sarasyn moche harme cytezeyns rage sette trybutes dyuerse demaundes ofte ben bondemen haue thyse thynges good ostages helde theyr childeren fowle ben seruage made bere donge fylthe fowle werkes herof rage moche greuyd cam fore bawdwyn kneled hym foot prayd hym ioyned handes right humbly wepyng grete teres wold delyuer fro turk forsayd suche wyse myght recouure theyr childeren helde shamefully bawdwyn wold fayne doo theyr request theyr desire theyr first requeste gete theyr loue thanke dyde arme hym alle myght haue yssued toun cam fore famosete assaylled toun moche vygorously within deffended men wel garnysshed strong place whan bawdwyn ben wote many dayes sawe coude lightly taken lefte fortresse nyghe knyghtes put garnyson men armes vytaylles commanded euery day shold renne fore toun famosete suffre yssue toun neyther man ne beste cam agayn rage cytezeyns toun sawe wel bawdwyn moche curtoys man wyse noble valyaunt alle thynges despyte gre e desdayne old duc whiche nought worth moche sorowe felaw lord toun therfor toke counseyl emonge sente puyssaunt man whiche many fortress montaynes named constantyn acorded alle gydre slee duc wold make bawdwyn duc lord vpon ffor moch hated old man without fayll greued log tyme many maners toke fro gold sylu plesyd hym toun ther none hardy durs withstade hym ne displese hym ffor yf dide ano turkes acqueynted made destroye theyr vygnes fruytes brenne theyr whete corne lede away theyr beestes yf ony went toun fere lese theyr heedes toun rage slewe theyr duc chees bawdwyn theyr lord capo lxxxjo forgeten wronges iniuryes suffred theyr duc hoped al yf deed thad bawdwyn shold deffende better therfore wente al armed enterprised vnto tour laye began strongly tassayle enuyronned round duc sawe peple sore meuyd angry hym called bawdwyn prayd hym take tresour moche wolde repease peple bawdwyn cam emong trauaylled moche prayer menace haue supposed haue repeased myght doo nothyng ffor alway ther cam moo suche wyse companye encreced bawdwyn departed then fro spak duc said shold take hym suche counseyl myght eschewe furye peple ffor myght remedye thenne duc man despayred bonde corde wyndowe descended doun therby whan apperceyued thurgh smeton arowes er myght come therthe thenne toke hym al deed drewe hym thurgh toun smote heed coude doo ynowgh satisfie theyr crueltees morn toke bawdwyn force ayenst deffendyng hym self lyft hym vp theyr kyng lorde made hym oth feaulte delyuerd hym grete fortresse toun gaf hym rychesses moche grete tresours grekes assembled long tyme thus cyte rage delyuerd withoute contradiction bawdwyn banduc lord ffamosete sawe bawdwyn conquerd alwey londes contrees encreced puyssaunce sente hym messagers whiche lete hym wete cyte moche stronge myght lightly wonne wold selle hym yf wold gyue hym x besauntes bawdwyn aduysed hym herupon counseyl acorded bye payd hym receyued toun entierly banduc rendred thostages holden alle thenne thus conquerd hertes loue toun called hym theyr fader dyde alle plesyd hym theyr power redy tobeye hym deth bawdwyn wente assieged toun serorge nygh rage tokeit ordenaunces capo lxxxijo londe cyte named serorge wherin dwellyd none peple sauf hethen men lord toun named balak turkes therin dyde many traueyls vylaynous oultrages many prayde bawdwyn theyr lord loue god thaffection wold take counseyl sette remedye thyng answerd two cytees one named fynemyne terme dyde ought doo cause londe theyr enemyes assured ouermoche suche wyse nyght grete partye turkes espyed smote sodanly began slee theyr beddes neuertheles somme ther apperceyued ran theyr armes cam ayenst turkes sold theyr lyf dere thende alle slayn none escaped alle thoost except thre foure atte moste vntrew greek latyus departed fraudelously fro h moo thensample hym capo lxxxxvij latyus disloyal greek haue spoken fore themperour delyuerd oure peple lede conduyte soynously taken heede gouernaunce thoost vnto day rewle baron alway peyned hym deceyue alle maners myght apperceeued wel thaffayres thooste good poynt ne good disposicion doubted moche ful cowardyse thought pylgryms shold somme day surprised turkes toun shold alle slayn therfor spak secretely one counseylled leue siege al thooste shold departe cytees men helde vnto newe tyme ffor certayn sayde themperour sente gret est hooste myght assemble come socoure sone myght fynde grasse erthe horse hym self cause loued werke oure lord noble men wold eterprise vpon hym comyn prouffyt grete tr uayll hym self wold goo dylygently themperour robaste hym hoost alle vytaylle myght fynde make hym come many baron knewe vpon poynt falsenes apperceyued sought manere waye flee byleuyd hym acorded shold goo waye made semblaunt retourne come sone ageyn lefte pauyllons som men pereaduenture sayd shold folowe come ellys yt neraught myght come thus departed deuyl brought lad hym away agayn ffor wordes sowen thensample departyng began many men departe fro thoost toke regarde theyr auowe ne oth promysed wente secretely one another famyne moche grete thooste baron conde fynde remedye ne counseyl therfore trouth sente ofte two two grettest lordes grete companye men pourchasse vytaylles wente moch surely landes theyr enemyes right deep ferre sleyng many wold haue deffended theyr passage vytaylles brought none ffor turkes contre apperceyued oure peple wente secke vytaylles ledde away alle theyr beestes theyr vytaylles vnto montaynes deserte place none myght come somme hydde wodes caues vnder erthe whiche men coude fynde prelate hoost counseylled doo penaunce tappese god thordenaunces made teschewe synne capitulo lxxxxviijo famyne mortalyte many peryllys cessed renne peple oure lord noble wysemen thoost trewe good relygyous bisshop puy legate oure holy fader pope spak gydre thenne sayd moche drede doubte lord angry pylgryms synnes therfor aduysed wold speke baron make pea acorde vnto lord ordeyned consentement alle thoost shold faste prayer penauce crye mercy vnto lord space iij dayes thende wold pardone theyr trespaces beholde pyte grete wepyng wayllynges herte commanded alle comyn wymmen euil lyf shold voyded cast thoost cryed thurgh al hooste taken adulterye fornycacion shood haue heed smeton incontinent droncardys tauernes player dyse grete othes deffended vpon payne fals mesures thefte alle suche thynges commaunded lefte eschewed choosen wise men trewe shold take heed punnysshe malefactours thyse ordenaunces statute somme founden culpable punnysshed therfore chastysed therby whan peple amended vnto lord mercy lord cam without taryeng ffor duc godeffroy whiche surete thoost theyr estandart ben longe seke thoccasion hurte taken londe pysside bere hath sayd fore nygh lytil anthyoche sodenly come good helthe wherof alle thooste moche grete ioye byleuyd fermely theyr penaunce prayer lengthed lyf respyted buymont fonde subtil remydye delyuer purge hooost espyes turkes capo lxxxxixo grete renommee spradd thurgh al thoryent toward contrees south ouer grete nombre peple contrees sonne goth doun comen besieged noble cyte anthyoche hit grete thyng trouth tydynges moche gretter withoute comparyson eueryche puyssaunt lordes countrees londes sente theyr espyes hoost ther many cessed come goo continuelly vnnethe myght ony thyng sayd thooste ne lodgys auon knowen panemye easy thyng peple ther turkes coude speke greek langage ermenye toke thabyte surreyens grekes hermeny ther many suche maner peple baron toke couseyl emog myght voyde purge thoost pestelence espyes ffor helde grete paryll grete dauger theyr couyne purpoos shold knowen lo de theyr enemyes light thynge knowe suche espyes emonge alle thynges coude fynde none remedye holde theyr counseyl secrete fro forthon saye lasse peple woont doo buymont whiche moche grete wytte hye hert spak baron sayd manere ffayr lordes praye ye wil late cheuysshe matere ffor haue remembryd shal delyuerd peryl wherfor praye gyue charge therof baron helde buymont moche wyseman prudent gladly sette charge therof hym departed fro counseyll buymont forgate promysed whan tyme soupper cam disposed ordeyned hym souppe made knyghtes contre take somme turkes prison made theyr throtes cutte smote pyeces arrayed rosted thenne began demaunde wold doo thenne buymont sayd men ad men also saye alle baron thus ordeyned sworn alle espyes myght taken thost shold rosted secuyd table baron baron shold ete oth thyse tidynges anon spred thurgh thoost suche iustyce lodgys buymont alle men ran theder see merueylle turkes self comen thoost espye moche affrayed euerych thought longe departed fro lodgys cause doubted shold seruid lyke wyse aftir whan retorned home lordes sent sayd tolde al aboute countrey suche men come tassiege anthyoche suffred moche mesease harder ayenst trauayll laboure stone yron cruelte passed alle beres lyon ffor wylde beestes te men alle rawe thyse men roste afore deuoure tydynge suche wyse knowen publysshyd alle paynemye soudan grete admyrals myght neuer fynde man wolde come espye hoost cyte assyeged effrayed grete hydour fro tyme afterward counseyl baron better kept secretely fore caleph egypte sente messagers grete ftes vnto hoost capitulo co emong mescreauntes grete lordes prynces caliphe egipte moost myghty men moost ryche goodes sente messagers vnto baron thoost shal saye occasion grete hate moche fiers hath hen bytwene turkes thoryent turkes egypte hath auncyent long tyme cause discorde theyr creaunce mysbyleue eche sayd yet doo fals sarasyns haue sayd fore begynnyng book therfore ben ofte warre somtyme one partye aboue another tyme tyme peple fore anthyoche caliphe speke helde alle londe egypte vnto cyte sureye whiche conteyneth wel xxx iourneyes longe soudan perse lytyl tofore oure peple cam conquerd toun anthyoche wy che royame egypte alle londe entierly vnto braas seynt george haue sayd fore calyphe egipte moche suspection sowdan perse moche plesyd hym destruction dommage moche ioye solyman lost nycene whiche solyman neuew sayd soudan enfebled men also e plesyd cristen peple besieged cyte anthyoche therfor sente good messagers speke whiche brought right grete yeftes moche ryche presentes yf wold receyue sayde caliphe redy gyue socoure ayde right largely men good vytayll prayd moche derely wold mayntene contenue theyr siege baron hoost receyued noble men comen sent hym honorably made soiourne wyse knewe anon wyt e vygour baron begonne haue moche grete doubte suspection peple valyaut yet sholde grete dommage theyr londe deuysed thyng ye shal mo redyng hoolly book ancean lord anthyoche baron sente vnto turkes theyr neyghbours demaunde socours capo cjo lord anthyoche grete noble men toun seyng men suffred moche famyne mesease haue sayd fore alle thyse thynges wol wyse leue theyr siege shewed theyr countenaunces trauayl greued wherfore moche abasshyd thenne ancean counseyl men moost pryue hym sente messagers lettres moost ryche neyghbours prayd hym right derely honour theyr lawe sauyng self loue wold come socoure without taryeng sente word maner shold approche secretely anthyoche shold couere busshement nygh abyde pylgryms like ben acustomed suche tyme shold come brydge ffor shold sprynge toun shold assaylle whyle besy fyghtyng embusshed shold sodenly breke come hynde fyght shold enclosed bytwene within withoute suche wyse none shold escape herd thise lettres thyse messagers doubted moche oure peple wherfor acorded gladly counseyl assembled hallape cezayre haman cytees tyl grete nombre peple dyde moost secretely myght commaunded began departe approuche anthyoche cam castel named harant whiche fro then xiiij myle lodged thought morn sone scarmuche shold bytwene pylgryms toun shold smyte theyr spore vpon oure men oure cristen men grete peryl one thyng ther thenne tho tymes dyde grete
