apperceyued day armed made vj bataylles ef turkes sente fore corrours cam sayde grete peple cam ayenst sente fore ij theyr bataylles aftir cam grete peple whan approuched grete desraye archer approuched first whiche shotte thycke oure men smote speres moche asprely suche wyse made flee chaced theyr grete bataylles suche destrayt bytwene ryuer laye myght sho ene flee theyr customme medlyng grete fiers baron men armes dyde moche wel turkes lost maner fyghtyng myght deffende ne endure strok oure peple fled e theyr way al th myght thenne whan baron sawe began doo wel commaun ed noman shold faygne folowe chaas asprely turkes fledde vnto bernant oure n folowed alwey sleyng bewyng heedes armes al waye passed wen dede men chaas endured wel x myle turkes within castel hernant sawe theyr men cam alle discomfyted sette fyere castel self fledde hermyns cristen men many castel recouuerd fortresse yelded oure men whan cam daye slayn turkes moo ij thousand toke v c heedes best arrayed brought opene tydynges theyr comyng alle armed redy make thassaylle brydge alle incontiyent whan shold see whan sawe nyght passed day cam without hauyng ony knowleche theyr approuchement theyr espyes made cause oure men fought shold abasshed thoccasion theyr peple shold come oure peple approuched turkes apperceyued abode discomfyted cause oure men cam ioyously alle theyr despoylles thenne aroos sorow fortresse largely thenne alle thost assured ben within walles good cyte siege endured thenne v monethes shippe genewes cam theder whiche brought pylgryms vytaylles aryued porte sette ryuer helle therfor durst none goo without grete companye baron aduysed make grete fortresse thende brydge mahommerye turkes wold sette men armes kepe deffende thyssue brydge yf turkes wolde come cause peple knyghtes moost noble lye wayte theyr retornyng happed fourth day men sette way rotorne brought armures many horse laden vytaylles thynges toke none heede laye wayte turkes brake sodenly surprised oure busshes fledde montaynes woodes toke none heed brought whan baron sawe knewe wel theyr strengthe lyke theyres began come lodgys dylygently many men myght conduyte wold folowe ne myght alle slayn slayn haue slayn valyaunt men grete counseyl ye sente see f de perysshed also felaws shold haue conduyted see two wayes one deye good criscen men world certeyn receyue reward ihesu criste shal serue vnto without aduenged vnderstande ye shal saye semeth thyse turkes yf haue victorye vpon oure men sayd shal mounted grete pride grete bobance angre v wyl come cyte brynge theyr proyes fardellys fore v ye shal wel see shal kepe wel ordenaunce shal goo folyly shal grete auantage v therfore counseyll yf hold v alredy doo seruyse oure lord ffor whiche departed oute oure countrees late v haue hym stedfast hope ffor guerdonneth right wel souldyours whan enemyes shal come v late v receyue vygorously glayues speres swerdes late eueryche remembre wel herte wronge shame haue oure lord oure self worde duc sayde wel vnderstande alle plesyd merueyllously well began warne eche somone doo well knewe gydre helde al redy thenne buymont aryued cam emong lytil whyle cam therle tholouse tolde theyr mesauenture moche grete ioye comyng escaped moche comforted eche sayd counseyl duc godeffroy acorded therto sayd ought doo abode alle gydre ancean capytayn cyte thyse semblaunces sawe knewe peple discomfyted oures moche doubted theyr comyng agayn cause men yssued ayenst therfor e dyde crye toun alle men shold arme come yate brydge redy araye socoure peple yf nede men sente espyes theyr courreurs dyuerse partyes tenquyre knowe whan turkes shold come fro parte batayll men auenged turkes stroke duc godeffroy gaf bataylle capo cvo longe whyles taryed theyr hertes desyryng doo prowesse yf tyme place theyr al abasshed thenne began smyte asprely right syde lyft flewe presse suche wyse euery man wold best moost valyaunt moche gaf theyr enemyes leyser aduyse shold doo myght endure grete strengthe oure men wold haue drawen toward brydge duc godeffroy moche kn suche thynges pouru yed therof fore taken lytil ritoire whiche ayenst brydge helde hym bataylle alle turkes chaced ward hym slewe made retorne knyghtes noble men theyr countrees dyde meruaylles armes ther neuer man lyuyng sawe ony werk better enterprised e valyauntly achyeuyd communely alle ancean sawe bataylle grete sawe peple yssue gyue herte courage put awaye thesperaunce theyr flyght commaunded shette yates cam pryckyng ayenst oure men wold haue made theyres retorne whiche discomfyted affraye drede grete neuer made semblaunt therto self frely cam whan sawe prowesse men grete stroke gaf torned theyr backes ne neuer made grete resistence fyghtyng grete merueyllous betyng doun turkes men myght grete payne passe ther grete noyse grete crye terryble neyhyng horse oueral shold haue herd thondre made yates slette ofte day peryl lese theyr lyues wyues turkes maydens feble peple toun vpon walles tourette sawe theyr peple torne ynowgh wen wherfor loue grace alle companye gaf brother duc alle thyssues londe side ryuer eufrates gaf hym cyte tor besel contre ther wherin moche whete wyne oyle yet aboue al gaf hym l besauntes noble man hermonye whiche named nycose whiche wel acqueynted bawdwyn loue sente vnto duc godeffroy pauyllon moost fayr moost ryche myght wher seen ouer straunge facion merueyllously grete whan messagers bare haoste one pancrace moche ryche man hermonye haue spoken fore dyde espye waye dyd take sente pauyllon buymont presented hym name whan seruauntes nycose cam duc godeffroy told hym alle pancrace hym therof moche grete desdayne syth toke hym erle fflaundres loue acqueyntaunce ony baron wente buymont demaunded pauyllon gyuen hym buymont answerd therof knewe longyng hym ffor noble man coutre gyuen hym whan knewe duc wold suffre hys curtosye atte prayer requeste baron rendred delyuerd hym sayd pauyllon thende noyse shold sourde ne arryse bytwene myght lette werke oure lord thus good frendes many men merueylled valyaunt man duc godeffroy thynge founden reprehended meuyd ayenst hye noble man lytil thyng pauyllon ne see none reason noble herte maye suffre shame late hym vnderstande shold hym grete shame also shold ayenst honour yf suffred taken away hym ffor couetyse dyde erle estyeuen chartres bloys fledde fro hooste shamefully capitulo cixo renommee rded moche grete grewe euery day soudan perse whiche ryche puyssaunt request anthyoche doo somone peple alle power f r come socoure cyte assembled merueyllous grete peple ffor tydynge cam thooste sayd many men yssued cyte come thooste hermyens surryens whiche cristen wherof happed steuen therle chartres bloys whiche noble puyssaunt wyse wysdom baron thooste named hym fader couseyl made hym self seke sayd toke leue frendes bycause sayde wold goo allexandrye lasse whiche nyghe porte wold abyde til deed ellys hool thus departed lad away hym grete good hym departed iiij men whiche companye countreye wente strayt allexandrye lasse helde hym thende yf oure peple vyctorye bataylle whiche wayted dayly wold retorne thoost guarysshyd hool maladye yf meshapped anon wold haue entred shippis whiche alle redy retourne countrey thynge alle baron thooste abasshed angry wepte hoote teeris pyte hye noble man toke none hede gentilnesse wytte ne worshyppe men dyde hym departed euyl poynt many men shame withdrawe hym thus departed many baron counseyl gydre dyde crye thurgh hooste noman shold hardy departe withoute leue ffor yf ony wente shold holden murdyrere iustyce shold doon suche men ordenaunce teschewe payne kepe theyr honour held pea thoost obeyed alle pee hooste obeyed debonayrly baron thooste monkes cloystrers theyr abbot withoute departyng ony theyr companye cristen man emyrferins whiche anthyoche acqueynted hym buymont cao cxo anthyoche holy cyte haue spoken fore conuerted prechyng seynt peter thappostle alway helde wel fayth yet holdeth certaynly god thanked whan disloyalte falsenes mahomet thurgh thoryent cyte wold neuer receyue lawe whan myghty men countre wold constrayne force euyl lawe deffended well ayenst alle suche wherof happed whan deuyl sette false byleue thurgh alle londe perse vnto braas seynt george fro inde vnto spayne cyte abode alway fayth trouthe ihesu criste trouthe fourten yere fore peple cam theder grete soudan perse conquerd alle londes vnto anthyoche bycause myghty hold ony lenger yelded vnder puyssaunce grete man thenne cam oure men tassiege almost alle toune helde fayth oure lord withoute faylle power ne noo seygnorye cyte ffor medled nothyng sauf theyr craftes theyr marchaundyses wynne theyr breed turkes bataylles wente armes whan nede ther none hardy cristen men durst arme hym specially syth peple cam fore toun cristen therin holden suspect durst yssue ne goo oute theyr howses many suche cristen men grete lygnage moche shame lygnage noble men beremyens named theyr langage bam cyrra saye sone harbergyers certeyn langage descended theyr lygnages yet ben ther somme make hawberks toure whiche named tour two sustres toure ii bretheren lordes lygnage oldes name emerferyus moche sage prudent man acqueynted pryue lord toun suche wyse made hym notarye within palays man herde men speke moche good buymont fro begynnynge siege wel vnderstode comyn renommee wyse man trewe grete herte enterpryse therfore sente hym messager acqueynted hym moche pryuely lete hym knowe alle beyng state cyte purpoos turkes bothe two wysemen ther coude wel couere theyr counntenaunces fewe peple buymont knewe hym somme deuyses sayd emyrferius sente buymont maner acorded delyuer hym toun cao cxjo seuen monethes tho endured siege fore toun buymont wyse subtil many tymes essayed frende toun cyte myght yolden cristen men ofte sente hym sone sayd thus hym manere fayre swete syre trowe certaynly lord ihesus criste wold acqueyntaunce loue ffor euer syth haue acqueynted myn herte neuer rested drawe acorde euery day bounte maner plesyd moche haue veray ferme fast hope myne shal yet tyme comynge moche holpen honoured thynge ye haue discouerid haue ben merueyllously pensyf syth haue herd haue moch counterpeysed wayes one side ffor thynke wel certeynly yf maye delyuer countrey fro peple ben enemyes oure lord rendre delyuere seygnorye fayth shal haue grete guerden oure lord grete honour world yf happed thus werke discouerd haue enterprised fore er cam ende conclusion shold delyuerd alle tormentes world alle lygnage effaced destroyed neuer shold spoken neuertheles many thynges put aduenture therfore wylle discouere alle herte hym hold trewe frende yf baron companye wylle graunte trewe men cyte shal youres euermore heyres yf may conquerd shal put aduenture shal delyuer tour holde whiche moche strong wel garnysshed shal doo goddes loue youres yf entende euery man shal haue part thyng goten warre therupon wyl laboure ne doo payne ffor wote neuer ende shold come therfor pray fayr swete syre trew frende ye put deuoyr payne toun youres couetyse prouffyt cyte cristen promyse day shal knowe shal thus graunted shal delyuer entree toun alway one thynge saye certayn yf made within short tyme ye shal neuer day world recouere ffor euery day come lord toun lettres messagers certefyeng come socoure toun ben ryuer eufrates whiche ferre ben wel ij c men armes yf come one syde cyte ye may suffre ne withstande ye shal alle deed taken therfore take ye vpon hasty counseyl buymont discouerd thynge duc godeffroy hu mayne duc normandye therle fflaundres capitulo c xijo fro day buymont herd began tenanyre moche subtylly examyne hertes baron demaunded otherwhyle wold doo cyte yf taken ansuer somme thought fer therfore taryed buymont discouere herte thought til sawe better poynt tyme neuertheles drewe part duc godefroy huon de mayne duc normandye therle fflaudres sayde trusted moche oure lord yf cyte myght graunted hym myght wel short tyme conquerd acorded moche preysed theyr courage wytte man wylle accomplysshe grete thyng thaccord thyng discouerd therle tholouse ansuerd wold neuer yf cyte taken gyue parte another man baron prayd hym moche wold consente therto nothynge therfor thynge suche daunger almost thynge alleloste ffor buymont put payne ne frende toun wold yf toun shold alle neuertheles alle buymont sente hym ofte grete yeftes kepe hym acqueyntaunce loue begonne bytwene grete socours soudan perse sente nthyoche c hagat assyeged rage capitulo cxiijo whyle thyse thynges ran thus anthyoche messagers fro ancean goon soudan perse demaunde ayde retorned wel theyr thynges ffor grete prynce atte requeste anthyoche atte prayer men enterprysed efface destroye alle pylgryms theder comen ther fore sente theder grete plente turkes cordyns countre delyuerd alle seygnorye gouernau ce hooste one acqueynted ffor trusted moche wytte loyalte prowesse man named corbagat commaunded alle men obeye hym sente lettres pendantes oueral londes commauded shold delyuerd ouer shold lede shold goo alle commaunded shold doo without contradiction departed fro countrey alle peple power passed ferre cam countre rage ther told hym one baron ffraunce helde cyte rage conquerd alle londe therof grete despyte sayd fore er passed ryuer eufrates shold take toun destroye alle fren themen shold fynde within bawdwyn lityl courage wel herd tydynges peple wel garnysshed cyte armes vytaylles noble men doubted lytil comynge ne menace ne grete wordes thyse peple reported hym corbagat commaunded cyte rage shold assieged dyde crye assault grete peyne dyde wenyng haue taken cyte alle therin kept toun deffended moche wel suche wyse endommaged moche without within loste thynge helde toun thre wekes worship ne prouffyt laste grete noble men thooste cam hym sayde counseylled hym departe fro siege ffor ought fyrst thyng whiche cam saye take slee alle fore anthyoche retornyng morowtyde shold haue toun rage bawdwyn yf deed shold take bynde hym presente hym theyr lord sheep moton h acorded theyr counseyl departed fro then allewaye taryeng turkes made sauyd oure prlgryms ffor mater acorded bytwene buymont frende yf comen strayt anthyoche oure men ben ouer grete meschyef bytwene brought turkes toun men beyng aduertysed grete hoooste corbagat sente somme theyr knyghtes esteme reported seen cao cxiiijo tydynges began strongly growe people cam merueyll yf effcayed hooste pylgryms baron assembled counseyl ordeyned comyn acord somme theyr wysemen vnderstode suche thynges esteme peple felde shold goo knowe couyne chosen dreues de nelle clarembault de venduel euerard de cherysy renard therle toul ledde knyghtes knowen preuyd armes departed fro thoost ferre approuched turkes sawe folowed fro fer neuertheles wel apperceyued lyke water renneth see cam fro alle partes grete rowtes merueyllous plente peple hooste corbagat thise noble men wente ferr sawe knewe alle theyr beyng rengthe syth drewe baron sayd trouthe baron prayde deffended also dere werk oure lord wold discouere thyng foote men thoost wyse kepe secrete fro ffor shold grete peryll yf knewe trouth shold flee away nyght alle despayr counseyl peple toke ordeyne theyr nedes whan knewe comyng right grete hooost cao cxvo baron toke counseyl faites burthon werke laye myght conteyne greuo poynt whiche som ther gaf counseyl shold departe fro siege somme horsbak foote shold abyde kepe toun shold mowe ioyne somme best horsed shold lede foote grete partye ayenst corbagat fyght ayenst hym thyng grete doubte wyste accorde buymont whan sawe surprised called duc godeffroy therle fflaundres huon de mayne duc normandye therle tholouse syth sayd thise wordes fayr lordes see moche grete doubte merueyl ffor comynge puyssaunt man cometh v bryngeth hym grete plente enemyes ne ye yet acorded maner ye shal attende ne shal countenaunce whan shal come ne saye semeth ng way may moche auaylle ffor yf yssue alle ayen turkes lyke somme men counseylle somme one partye abyde counseyl haue loste payne oure dispencis siege toun ffor sone shal departe fro hen alle half comen shal sende toun grete plente vytaylles fresshe men put yf noman abyde siege shal good doo yf ther abyde parte shal leue ffor whan alle gydre vnnethe maye constrayne toun thenne fewe shal abyde may haue force myght ayenst within therfor thyncketh muste seche remedye connseyl may fynde maner cyte maye yolden v may within fore er thyse turkes come shal sure thyng yf ye demaunde maye shal shewe way manere shal wel semeth haue frende cyte trewe man wyse apperceyue haue couenauuted gydre wherfor ought delyuer tour moche strong wel garnysshed alle nedeth whiche holdeth whan shal demaunde hym muste gyue hym thus doyng grete partye good hauoyr franchyses alyaunces muste kepe hym hys maye eche gyue ouer part quyte hym ony part cyte shal abyde myn heyres euermore ffor wyse entendeth shall delyuer hit yf plese maner ye may haue toun yf ye wil graunte somone warne fore suche wyse thyse couenautes wel accomplysshed godes grace yf plese ye maye fynde ony maner redy tacquyte alle parte one another oure companye yf wyl delyuer v cyte god knoweth shal plese wel shal right ioyous good fayth buymont declared fayte alle hooste acorded toun shold sauf erle tholouse capitulo cxvjo whan baron herd grete ioye theyr hertes anon acorded buymont requyred euery man graunted part shold quyte therof except therle tholouse whiche reuerrye wheryn sayde wold acquyte part ne gyue oner noman lyuyng baron promysed certeynly holde gaf hym fayth shold discouere noman prayd hym wold wysely brynge mater aboute dylygently laboure taccomplisshe ffor grete peryll myght come taryeng counseyl departed thus buymont wyse trewe spak messager knewe theyr couyne sente hym frende bad hym saye baron graunted hym toun shold hoolly moche glad chere therfor somoned hym fayth shold accomplysshe next nyght hooly promysed hym one thynge happed day moch helpyng werke thaccomplisshyng therof ffor frende buymont named emyrferyus entremedled moche thaffayres thynges ancean toun day whan besy werke sente sone tho grete hows fetche somwhat whan cam tour hastely founde one grete admyrals toun pleyed deled moder whan sawe grete sorowe erte ran agayn fader told hym lyke e founden fader moche wyseman moche sore angry sayd thyse wordes sone fayr sone semeth ynowgh thyse fals houndes take fro v alle haue kepe v fowle seruage b doo v alle shame maye ayde ihesu crist byleue shal laboure doo payne fynde maner whiche theyr power myght shal lassed mynuysshed shorted shal haue guerdon euyl haue v made thenne semblaunt angre sente sone buymont anon maner acustomed goo badde hym shold redy ffor hym wold hold hym nyght alle couenauntes badde hym also alle baron thooste shold yssue oute abeut none euery man armed bataylle make semblaunt goo ayenst corbagat begynnyng nyght retorne agayn pryuely withoute noyse kepe armed redy doo shal sayd aboute mydnyght buymont moche ioyous whan herd message aftir ledde hym fore baron thyng discouerd made hym saye theyr presence wordes brought baron whan herd hym moche ioyous sayd wel counseyl good faythful grete courage acorded therto anthyoche fere treson assembled counseyl whiche emyrferius deposed capitulo c xvijo one thyng happed toun acustomed ofte come grete werkes kepyng charge toun began haue suspection within theyr hertes deuyned cyte shold trayed knewe reson ne ne apperceyued grete semblaunce alway one spak grete men semed shold falle moche aroos murmur wordes assembled fore ancean lord toun told hym men fere without reson ffor cristen men toun doubte dommage myght come cyte ledde ancean wordes made hym aferd also anon sente hym named emyrferyus told hym worde ranne cause helde hym wyseman demaunded counseyl wold gyue sharp entendement apperceyuyng knewe anon lord demaunded thyse wordes knowe yf shold answere ony thyng whiche shold suspecte knewe wel assemblee made cause suspection thought wel brynge wenyng answere sayd fayr lordes ye hye noble wysemen ye ought conne good thancke lord specially ymagyne doubte trayson ffor grete thyng ye haue kepe ought doubted alle may falle ffor peryll lyues oure franchyses wyues chylderen herytages thise ben thynges ought well vnderstanden kepte semeth two wayes maye gyuen counseyl thyng suche wyse yf ony vntrew suche ttaytre wold destroye countrey shold haue power thynge myght ne spoken haue toures kepyng therfor thynketh yf ye haue suspection ye may wel remedye ofte remeuyng fro theyr place ffor thynge may deuysed moche grete leyser whan ye chauge thus ofte suche wyse nyght shal sette next nyght fer then shal haue knowleche ye shaltake fro alle ease commune speke ony trayson whan herd cou seyl cristen man emyrfery gaf acorded alle well therto fylle alle suspection fro theyr hertes ayenst thus deuysed shold haue yf ben late nyght grete remeuyng myght made space tyme lord commaunded kepe alle cyte hoolly thus departed fro counseyl emyrferyus sawe wel thynge enterprised yf buyuont hasted shold neuer take good ende therfor thought moche brynge purpoos effect without ony man shold perceyue meschyef turkes made euery daye cristen men anthyoche enhabytyng cao cxviijo fro begynnyng cyte assyeged turkes toun grete suspection grekes surryens heremyns generally alle cristen men duellyd anthyoche wherof happed poure cristen men theyr howses garnyson sufficiant longe tyme made voyde toun alle theyr meyne ffor wold cyte charged ne encombred ret yned ryche men within cause vytayll ynowgh kepte strayte fals occasion robbed euery daye toke fro alle theyr thynges chaced labour werkes toun yf walles make amende bare stone morter sande yf wold adresse engyns caste stone instrumentes warr muste drawe cordes neuer longe fo de cristen men fought none doo suche werkes whan trauaylled longe stede rewardes ledde bete thurgh stretes suche wyse leuer haue ben caste toun atte begynnynge receyued thyse fals houdes thus greued toun cristen thus acorded viij dayes fore speke emyrferyus frende buymont wolde slee alle cristen men yf one admyrals toun etted empesshed alway pryue frende cristen men made delaye vij dayes reason ffor sayd fayr sir hope cristen men haue assieged v shal departe fro siege viij dayes doubte corbagat cometh yf departe shal slee cristen men ben toun yf departe thenne maye ye doo ye haue deuysed thyse viij dayes passed suche wyse commaunded moche pryuely charge shold lee nyght thene day none cryed thurgh hooste pylgryms alle horse armed drawe euery man bataylle constituted ordeyned doo theyr capytayns shold commaunde men foote knewe nothyng shold doo ne horsmen neyther sauf buymont aduertysed thus departed fro thoost alle ordenaunce semed wel wold goo ferre wente forth tyl nyght whan derke commaunded shold retorne agayn secretely without ony noyse shold holde armed theyr lodgys valyaunt man emyrferius haue spoken fore brother hym suche courage good man sayd nothynge hym purposed doo ffor doubted moche wold agreable therto gydee tour hour none whan th bataylles yssued thooste behelde batayllementes emyrferyus wold preue knowe courage broder whiche yonger sayd hym fayr swete broder haue moche grete pyte thyse hyemen thou seest ffor oure creaunce moche faythful good cristen men ryde also surely yf ought nothyng doubte deth ful nygh ffor may may resiste ayenst come ayenst toun yf knewe trowe wold take couseyl broder answerd moch folyssh pyte thou hast see grete musardye certaynly shold plese wel turkes nowe smeton alle heedes slayn alle thou seest departe alle lyke wyse ffor neuer syth entred londe neuer good day ne one good nyght haue made v suffre many euilles thoccasion comyng therfor may loue wold shold haue euyl endyng right soone whan emyrfery herd thyse wordes doubted fore saye broder purpoos fro forth doubted nomore began hate hym moche courage thought wel hym myght destroubled grete auauncement cristendom therfore grete anguysshe myght delyuer hym dilygence buymont made werke emyrferyus slewe brother delyuerd toun cristen men capitulo cxixo bvymont slepte nyght ffor shold haue ben moche displesyd yf neclygence werke shold taryed wente ofte baron knewe thynge counseylled helde honde laddre cordes moche subtylly made aboue shold fasted creucaux walle good stronge crochettes yron fastne also therthe whan cam aboute mydnyght toke messager knewe secrete pryuely sente hym frende knowe yf yet tyme shold approuche wally ffor hym thought alle cyte moche pea reste whan messager cam hym abyde stylle saye worde tyl mayster watc departed passyd ffor custome suche cyte aboue watche ordeyned aduysed noble wyseman shold serche vysyte euery nyght watche amende founde amys wente thus thre four tymes nyght grete companye peple bare light longe aft r cam sawe tour emyrferyus sawe alle thynges wel ordeyned good disposicion plesyd hym wel passed forth man sawe thenne tyme performe werke sayd messager goo thy way dylygently saye thy lord tyme doo well come fore tour see haue good companye hym trewe messager departed forthwith emyrferyus entred tour founde broder slepyng moche faste fere shold awake er werke accomplysshyd myght destrouble therfore toke swerd roof hym thurgh bothe sydes slewe hym messager cam buymont told hym erande cam incontinent fore tour baron hym knewe werke eche fewe good trew emyrferi put heed salewed resalewed hym aualed corde doun wall toke boude fast thed laddre cordes whan bounden drawen vp fa ned attached crochettes yron aboue none hardy wold fyrst goo vp whan buymont sawe toke thene laddre first valyaut man ardant ccomplysshe werke wente vp til cam batillement emyrferyus knewe anon buymont toke hym arme kyssed hys honde buymont wente vpon walle kysshed hym swetly thanked hym seruyse emyrferyus ladde hym towre sayde hym beholde see haue god man ye see deed brother germayn haue slayn hym cause wolde acorde werke ye haue enterprysed buymont moche grete ioye ffor fro thenne forthon knewe well frende dyde alle good fayth thenne cam creueuls put oute heede called peple sayd shold come vp dylygently laddre durst go vp alway supposed deceyuaunce buymont moche valyaunt iust put doun foote laddre descended doun erthe sayd fayr lordes ye tarye ouer longe doubte ffor knowe ye certaynly good man hath shewde brother hath slayn loue v whan herd toke laddre myght best beste mounted vp many ther men ynowgh walle therle fflaundres went vp tancre tenseyne shold doo whan fyrst towr wel garnysshed men ranne slewe watche men helde toures mayntene cristen men pryse affraye turkes toun cao cxxo foote laddre abode somme baron conduyte thooste whan sawe vpon walles men ynowe myght garnysshe dyuerse towres ran hastely lodgys make peple arme drawe nerer thende myght al redy entre whan men walles ydle noble hardy wise anon x towres taken alle arenge slayn alle founde therin cyte yet meuyd ne waked ffor grete men toun whan herde noyse supposed certaynly slayn cristen men lyke commauded affraye none thynge meued oute theyr beddes partye oure goon vp posterne men walles descended brake vp locke opened yate suche wyse many entred oure peple cam grete gate called gate brydge alle watche kepte slewe opened gate squyer buymontys ran til cam hye towre whiche vpon tertre dongeo toun fyxed baner buymont lord whan oure peple toun apperc yued daye nyghe dawenyng appiered thenne made sowne theyr trompettes usynes calle al people hooste baron vnderstode signe smote h r spor entred yates whiche founde opene alle theyr bataylles foote men thooste wooke knewe nothyng counseyll sawe tentes empty voyde apperceyued toun taken thenne began hastely enne gayne suche wyse none abode turkes toun woke herde noyse sawe men armes thurgh stretes thenne apperceyued poynt began flee theyr howses lede theyr wyues chylderen whan fledde fro one rowte men ecountred another gretter whiche slewe alle surryens hermyeus cristen men toun apperceyued thyng wente moche grete ioye toke armes hastely wente forth men tolde place mooste peple tresours slewe turkes moche gladly payned moche rendre guerdon betynges tormentes thoost thene entred toun baron sette baners toures grete occision slaughter toun spared noman ne woman ne childe brak vp dores chestes ye shold haue seen gold syluer departed stretes semeth well thyng conquerd wonne warre shal make long deuyses ther slayn toun day moo xm bodyes laye alle bare wayes stretes ancean lord authyoche fledde posterne toun recountred put deth cao cxxjo whan ancean sawe cyte thus bytrayed peple myght escape fledde hye fortresse dongeon doubted moch goo theder ffor thought wel cristen men wold enuyrone incontinent tour yf entred therfor yssued posterne toun wente allone oute wytte ne knewe whether myght goo flee kepe hym whan wente thus feeldes moche ferre fro cyte certeyne hermyns mette hym knewe hym moche merueylled myght thought cyte taken approched hym lyke wold haue enclyned hym woonte thene toke hym smote hym doun therthe swerde smote heed bare toun presented vnto baron fore peple one maner peple comen athyoche toun come deffende theyr lawe souldyours prowesse armes gete honour pry thyse knewe wel leyng toun mouted vpon horse alle armed begonne renne ayenst hylle toward dongeon aduenture mette route men thus wente sechyng toun ran moche hardyly thyse maner peple wold haue eschewed smote theyr hors toward valeye fylle doun bancke suche wyse alle brused men hors harnoys abyllementes ther deed wel iij c som ther toun born whan apperceyued mornyng men within toke hors rode yates men opened ther oure men wente aftir sued brought many agayn put pryson som escaped ran vnto montaynes hour tierce whan toun serched peple assembled anon apperceyued alle toun vytayll wondre ffor siege thene endured nygh ix monethes moche peple ben therin duryng siege gold syluer preceo iewellis vessel dyuerse facions clothes sylke ryche tappet thynges foude moch eche alle charged moch myght bere cam wel poynt oure poure pylgryms fynde suche rychesse grete mesease suffred ther fouden toun v c good hors armes riyht lene wery thus cyte anthyoche taken yere thyncarnacion lord mlxxxxviij iij day moneth iuyn aftir men made grete slaughter theyr enemyes men helde counseyl take dongeon thene beyng seased turkes cao cxxijo pylgryms theder comen fro many coutrees grete labour thene ful shedyng blood enemyes baron assembled counseyl aduysed emonge werk yet parfyght ther yet trauayll peryll tyl dongeon taken goten whiche right stronge wel garnysshed walles toun sette good warde kepers alle yates dyde crye thurgh alle toun assault commanded shold come tour montayne whan cam theder knewe wel certaynly thynge lightly goten ffor fortresse myght goten famyne therfor trauaylled lytil withdrewe made peple retorne montayne aboue toun deuyded tweyne like sayd fore depe valleye whiche stepe plom doun syde whiche toward thoryent moch fayrer vpon playne wel brode ful northeste valeye deep semeth right helle hydous thynge beholde coude neuer ymagyned myght myned fro dongeon vnto toun way whiche strayt grete payne one man allone maye goo come baron acorded wold close litil terter waye thende dongeon shold mowe descende ne doo euyll ne harme oure men cyte made walle moche stronge lyme sonde whiche put men armes ynowe wel poynt sette walles stone engyns redy caste stone yf turkes descended cam doun baron wente toun take couseyl werkes ordeyned deuysed alle men shold retorne abyde newe walle tyl dongeon taken sauf duc godeffroye whiche comyn couseyl alle shold abyde kepe gate est fortresse men made withoute gate delyuerd buymont herde tydynges grete prynce corbagat haue spoken fore shold arryue shortly ffor thene entred londe anthyoche ac rded sholde countrey moche ioyous cyte handes pylgryms fayth hyd brought moch longe siege destroyed countre without emptyd toun within whyles thooste garnysshed toun somme thoost crobagat cam rennyng fore capo cxxiijo second day toun taken whyles oure peple entended garnysshe cyte cam thre honderd men hoost al poynt corbagat wel armed horsed vpon lyght horse see yf myght fynde ony oure men rode folyly countre embusshed alle sauf xxx beste horsed whiche cam fore toun began renne nycely drawe oure men arraye whan oure men sawe hey grete desdayne wende grete shame yf founde speke syth come fer fore noble man haue spoken fore hooste many prouffytes wytte prowesse named rogier de barneuylle companye duc normandye toke hym xv knyghtes e meyne cam toun ayenst turkes noble valyaunt hardy acustomed doo fayr fay te whan sawe smote hors spore ward cautele torned fledde men fo lowed hastely ferre launced vpon theyr watc e sprange oute embusshement ran vpon oure men ffor many wel proued armes rogier relyed ly til felawship cam deffendyng hym toward toun whan nyghe turke garnysshed stronge bowe smote rogier thurgh body suche wyse fyl doun deed fore hors anon felaws withdrewe toun turkes descended vpon hym smote heed seeyng walles bare way heed thus departed toun yssued oute grete crye lamentacion grete losse toke body buryed ho norably grete sorowe porche chirche seynt peter baron compleyned moche aboue noble man beste knewe hym thyrde day getynge pryse anthyoche corbagat hoost arryued fore cao cxxiiijo atte thyrde day anthyoche taken grete prynce corbagat cam cyte mornyng sonne rysyng grete plente peple alle coutre myght seen fro hyest place toun couerd baron sawe moche peple herd saye theyr hoost encreced euery day passed brydge lodged hym bytwene laye ryuer helle whiche wel myle fro one grete plente knyghtes grete nombre tentes pauyllons grete playne wherof haue spoken fore anthyoche stondeth ne yet myght alle receyue many lodged terrytoryes whan corbagat thus thre dayes lodged hym thought ouer fer fro cyte counseyl wold ner dongeon whiche turkes helde ayde comforte thought put men toun yate vnder dongeon whan lodged partye comprysed fro yate eest west yate syde toun fayllyng turkes deuysed hat mornynge erly shold haue begonne agayn thassault two men shold haue comen ben nyght byfore longe rowte turkes departed fro thooste corbagat wote many poure pylgryms wente pourchasshyng yf myght fynde ony vytaylles countre toke brought alle state fore corbagat whan sawe moche despysed ffor armures feble bowes tree swerdes rusty gownes habillemens old roten thenne sayd corbagat desdayne thyse peple seme well men shold take away fro soudan perse empyre conquere londe thoryent thyse shold wel content payd yf breed gobet bacon bowes ben stronge ynowgh slee sparowgh shal saye ye shal doo ye shal lede bounden poynt vnto lord soudan hath sent v hether telle hym dar sore aferd thyse men comen hether ffor haue enterprysed begonne warre ayenst suche men may see late allone werke ffor shal abyde many shal efface destroye alle suche wyse shal nomore spoken neuer born thus ledde thoo cristen men vnto soudan wede wel haue honour sente soudan torned hym afterward shame hym thought light thynge vaynquysshe cristen men whiche yet wel assayed grete famyne mesease oure men suffred cyte anthyoche beyng assyeged alle sydes sayd corbagat capitulo cxxviijo alle partyes cyte thus assieged toun ne myght yssue pourchasse vytaylle euyl ease meschyef famyne aroos toun moche grete greuo deffaulte vytayll suche wyse ete camel ass horse yet toke werse thynges whan myght gete ffor founden deed hound catte ete delyciously stede grete delices ffor hongry wombes made dauger seche suche myght fylle grete hye noble men acustomed moche honoured shame come wher ete suche mete wente oueral moche fowlly demauded playnly neded ladyes gentil wymmen maydens alle langour hongre alle pale bene many compelled begge aske moche grete shame none myght haue harde herte shold haue grete pyte haue seen ther many men wymmen aduysed lygnage born suche courage ferme theyr hertes none anguysshe suffred hongre wold goo axe beed fro dore dore thyse peple hydde theyr howses somme knewe dyde yet somme socour ther many deyed hongre ete myght men see knyghtes valyaunt men fore stronge noble theyr werkes feble poure wente stretes lenyng staues theyr heedes enclynyng doun askynge breed goodes loue shold ye haue seen lytil childeren soke theyr moders pappes moders nothyng ete threwe doun stretes thende shold norysshe grete payne shold ye haue fou de one onely man emong moche peple sufficiently hym neded ffor yf ony gold syluer auaylled hym nothyng ffor founde mete bye baron hye prynces acustomed holde fayr courtes gyue mete drynke many men hydde cause none shold fynde etyng ne drynkyng gretter anguysshe theyr hertes famyne poure peple ffor mette euery day theyr knyghtes theyr men theyr countrees deyde hungre mete gyue long thyng recounte alle meseases meschyefs suffred within anthyoche whyles tempeste endured moche may wel sayd selde neuer shal ye fynde hystorye grete prynces grete hooste suffred suche anguyssh hungre turkes felyng men suche whiche hurte peryllously corbagat sente men armes slee maronners porte wherof oure men grete losse capitulo cxxxo ahan famyne grewe thus euery day anthyoche many toun leuer slayn abyde thus hongre put allexandrye lasse cao cxxxjo gvyllem de grateuylle fledde hym ca allexandrye lytyl foude steuen therl chartres anthyoche abode comynge fro daye daye ffor baron mene peple supposed wold remembre goo anthyoche thenne cyte ferre then named ffynemyne wold well holde couenaunte made socoure peple peple empyre ther cam companye wel xl pylgryms abyden londe grete hooste cause sekenes cause grete moche noble wysemen ymes ayenst wylle god shold enterprise conquere countrey shold departe lest losse myght peple folowed shold coduyte place shold delyuerd deth many tymes sayd manere neuer wold v ne byleue mayntene theyr reuerye ffor ther many emonge lytil reson self ben deed yf abyden ne myght doo none honour lord ne prouffyte therfor departed commaunded god whiche saue kepe haue nede ye syre whome bounden good fayth aduyse ye take counseyl wyse men fore ye goo ony ferther trouth ye moost hye man world al ye haue companye moche peple corbagat hath aboute anthyoche ayenst one hath seuen therfore myn oppynyon yf acorde fore men put grete aduenture ye retorne home agayn yf ye ap rouche haue achyeued theyr werke cyte ye shal fynde redy ner ye approuche shame vyle shal retorne fro whan ye nyg thise thynges haue acouted knowe wel thise valyaunt men also grete parte maye ye knowe good man ye delyuerd v wete ta tyn seruaunt whiche wyse trewe whiche departed fro v many defaultes apperceyued v whan sayd themperour moche ame yd thise wordes hym brother buymont named guyon whan herd therle stephen thus speke alle wroth angry half araged despyte sayde al hye sayd trouthe departed cowardes moo grete wordes guylle de gratemeuyl gentilman born lygnage courage wyf suster guyen made hym hold pea blamed hym cause spak ayenst therle steuen guyen forbare hym warnynges sayd erle themperour whiche wold haue goon socoured men retorned shortly cao cxxxiij vpon thyse wordes themperour herd wold cou seylled called baron alle acorded themperour shold retorne fro then wher withoute goyng ony ferther ffor thought bett r remeue peple withoute perylle hurte fyght grete meschyef ayenst corbagat meue ayenst hym hate warre alle londe thoryent byleuyd fermely wordes therle stephen doubted turkes slayn anthyoche wold thenne goo londe receyue cyte nycene alle londe bythynie whiche oure men delyuerd hym wold garnysshe whan departed fro then brente destroyed alle londe fro cryne vnto nycene side cause turkes shold folowe hym vytaylle began faylle hym muste retourne thus happed wordes grete man fowly departed fro baron themperour retorned cristen peple beyng anthyoche lost grete socours whiche myght haue comen alle theyr delyueraunce grete necessyte thenne consydered gyue vnderstonde themperour yet dyde deuoyre certaynly werke lord ffor yf emperour cam peple grete power men al fresshe reysed siege discomfyted turkes oure lord shold haue ben honoured ne thanked yf trauayll baron pylgryms suffred themperour come laste shold haue vyctorye theyr payne shold haue ben wel guerdonned therfor lord suffred themperour departed werke shold accomplysshed ye shal glory honour peple peple anthyoche beyng aduertysed herof discouraged corbagat enhaunced pryde cao cxxxiiijo renomee cam anthyoche theperour approched wordes therle stephen guyllem de gratemeuyll theyr felaws torned back alle sydes anguysshes thyse tydynges empoysonned alle put despayr thenne began curse erle stephen alle companye taken fro grete ayde crobagat knowleche themperour cam moch doubte comyng ffor grete thyng puyssaunce themperour certayn retorned wherof moch grete ioye herte risen moch fiers pryde ran asprely toun oure men toun abasshed semed wel ouer lord god alle forgete lete falle despayre wold endure trauaylle apperteyned defence cyte alle hydde theyr howses day happed buymont whiche alle power thoost doo men ffor thassaultes withoute forth thassaylles within forth dyde crye peyn deth alle shold come cam none sente men fete e theyr howses somone come none wold come oute abasshed thought shold doo atte laste sette fyre toun dyuerse place thenne yssued stretes grete rowtes buymont sawe sayd hem commaundement bad shold doo dyd worde sourded toun many knyghtes baron counseyl p yuely emonge wold yssue oute toun nyght leue pepole within wold doo best myght drawe porte entre vpon see duc godeffrey knewe word sente hastely bisshop puy alle baron grete partye knyghtes fylle theyr foot requyred loue god wold neuer thynke suche thynge ffor yf dyd god shold hate shold lefe theyr sowles men despayre mercy oure lord syde world shold lefe honour euer also theyr lygnage whiche nothyng forfayted shold shamed euer poynted fingre londes whiche yssued shold lasse renomed lasse preysed long world shold endure alle thise departynges myght neuer receyue good worde ne honoure thyse wordes prechyng bisshop puy loste euyl talente alle euyll purpops began affeble toun honger mesease suche wyse abode wylle oure lord ofte cam theyr remembraunce goodes rychesses grete eas lefte theyr countrees loue seruyse oure lord yelded suche guerdon deyed euery day honger kept hem fro thyse dogges cruel byleuyd hym slewe beheded despyte reprouche cristen fayth maner wold chyde recounte alltheir meseases lord alle werkes may forgete mercy sete grete cofort ffor clerk born prouynce named eter cam day bisshop puy therle tholouse sayd moche grete drede holy apostel seynt drew appiered hym thryes nyght slepyng warned hym shold goo baron saye speer lord percid syde crosse hyd chirch seint peter cyte place certainly shewd hym said wel yt come saye ne signefye seynt andreu menaced hym last tyme yf dide message shold meshappe body merueylle yf clerke doubted saye ffor poure man lowe lygnage lytil lettred thyse two hye men whan herd hym brought hym fore baron assembled merueyllous myracles dyde peple hath conquerd long syth wyll ayde oure lord vpon turkes haue holden wrong force certeyn tyme therfor thou oughtest suffre v enioye oure herytage retorne thou thy countrey yf thou wilt doo knowe thou certayn within thyrde day swerdes shal fynysshe ende debate thende thou complayne desire wille deth pourchasse moch peple comyn bataylle shal offre wete yf thou wilt fyght thyn owne persone shal sende ayenst one al hye prynce thou art thou shalt fyght whiche maye vaynquysshe ouercome shal conquere quarelle euermore withoute debate yf thynge plese take certayn lord gyuen vyctorye thenne shold retorne myght tarye take gadre despoylles corbagat fro begynnyng siege cyte alwaye doubte grete suspection tha peple shold sodanly come vpon hoost specially syth peter theremyte hym message therfor commaunded dongeon yf oure men thought yssue shold sowne busyne sette oute baner shold yssue wherof happed whan thyse bataylles renged fore yate fore yssued aboute houre pryme tour made signe like commaunded corbagat vnderstode men cam anon sente two thousend archiers brydge kepe shold passe whan turkes cam theder mayntene passage descended alle afoote yates opened oure men yssued thordenaunce deuysed huon mayne alle bataylle cam fyrst vn paas whiche kept enemyes archiers men foote taryed lytil myght passe wise whan huon noble man apperceyued smo e hors spore smote bothe sydes late turkes foote take theyr horse thenne torned fleyng defendyng shotyng bowes ancean de ribemont rode ayenst bete helde rowte short allone men cam hym myght come smyte emong delyuerd many oftymes plunged depe presse certaynly men supposed ben lost whan cam agayn discouerd hym wel made large place hym alle men bebelde hym gate moche grete honour pry huon le mayne forgate forgoten ffor whan thyse archiers disconfyted latynes cam theyr ordenaunce softe paas thenne began falle rayne dewe swete rousee neuer seen semed euery man verytably benediction lord grace heuen many thynges ffor withoute faylle oure men wold haue seygnorye dyde many ennoyes vylonyes theyr hostes within theyr howses erle hym self cause grete plente men hys owne countre called fewer lasse counseyll noble men cyte who helpe comen hyenesse noble lordship therof moch grete desdayne within hertes repented theinof chosen hym sette hym lord ouer ffor doubted therle whiche lyberall gaf euery man shold day take therfor sete admyrals turkes theyr neyghbours wold pourchasse gladly theyr helpe therle bawdwyn shold slayn atte leste put oute chassed awaye fro cyte suche wyse shold neuer retorne turkmans acorded wel werk mater ferforth rage toke alle theyr goodes pryuely sette howses theyr acqueynted neyghbours cytees castellys ther whyles spak aduysed treyson frende therle bawdwyn cam hym recounted fayt al longe merueylled moch therof dyde enquyre thyng founde soo knewe wel ordeyned trayson shold doo secretely sende men toke capytayns falsenes put theyr eyen theyr heedes moche trespaced chassed toun toke alle somme lete dwelle stylle cyte toke good moche myght gete wel thoccasion murdre thyse traytres deuysed xx besautes departed alle pylgryms holpen hym take castellys fortress somme cytees rage moche dradde doubted moche neyghbours suche wyse none durste enterprise ony debate ayenst hym grete hye men contre wold gladly haue pourchaced moyens maners delyuerd hym yf myght therle bawdwyn daunger deth e treson turk named balac capitulo cl countre grete hye man turk w named balac acqueynted moche pryue therle bawdwyn somtyme lord cyte arge fore peple cam coutre turke appe ce ued therle bawdwyn sayde hym alle counseyll wonte ne shewde hym good chere day cam hym shewde hym fayr langage shold fortresse whiche wold gyue hym delyu cause also wold haue nomoo ffor loue shold suffyse hym wold sende wy childeren rage dwell vnder hym cause sayde turkes neyghbours specially lygnage hated hym moche pourchassed alle harme myg grete acqueyntaunce cristen men erle thought nothyng alle wel sayd wold go requeste fortresse day appointed bytwene bothe therle cam theder honderd horsmen balac fore fals traytre hyd honderd men well armed within fortresse whan arryued fore fortresse balac prayd therle wold come vp hye see place stronge shold brynge fewe men hym ffor sayd certayn hynges myght take harme yf alle entred good erle wold haue doon soo company valyaunt knyght wel aduysed wise man whiche aduertysed felaws knyghtes grete perylle daunger lete hym goo wold suffre hym reteyned hym force ffor doubted moche malyce man suche wyse theyr hertes suspection treson erle abode counseyl sente vp xij men wel armed toure see yf ther ony thyng doubte helde hym emog men wente vp anon apperceyued wel trayson ffor turkes sprange oute theyr place hyd toke thise xij men force desarmed reteyned bounden handes foot whan erle knewe moche sorouful men thus lost thenne drewe hym forth spak balac moche prayd hym coniured hym feaulte oth made hym wold yelde men hym atte leste sette rawnson wold gyue moche wold haue balac answerd hym trauaylled nought ffor shold neuer haue none yf wold gyue hym cyte sororge whiche ben fore therle sawe fortresse lyghtly goten ffor ouer stronge stode stronge place rychely garnysshyd retorned rage moche anguysshous paryll whan wold thatycemet felo turk haue goon vp tour sorouful taken delyuerd cyte sororge kepe vnto moche wise valyaut good knyght named foubert de chartres man kept hit c men armes valyaut men whan herd saye lord ben thus almost bytrayed lost xij men sory thought myght helpe ayenst fals turk foot longe nyght sette busshement nygh vnto fortresse part men mornynge fewe companye cam fore toure toke proye beestes hye batayllemet sawe fewe told balak men fortresse toke ho s hastely folowed rescowe whiche droof awaye suche wyse exployted cam vpon thembusshement sprange sodanly oute closed foubert retorned vpon slewe wote many vj toke lyue ffor incontinent vj men helde fortresse longe aftir four escaped fortresse brake theyr prison whyles theyr kepars slepte whan balak sawe ther nomoo two dype smy e theyr heddes ffro forth therle bawdwyn acqueyntance dyuerse admycal aboute hym wold neuer acqueynte hym ne truste ony turk eschewed theyr companyes theyr amytee shewde wel sone ffor ther hye grete man turk contre named balduc haue spoken fore whiche sold auncyen cyte named samoloc vnto bawdwyn turk encouenaunted promysed shold brynge wyf childeren within rage sought fals occasion delaye thynge day cam bawdwyn acustomed doo bawdwyn demaunded hym dyde couenaunted promysed e egan excuse hym thynges trewe erle toke hym incontinent dyde smyte heed therle tholouse toke cyte albane ere constitued bisshop capitulo cliio duc godeffroy soiourned thus haue sayd lond torbesel therle tholouse assembled peple toke grete plente pour pilgryms ydle dyde nought wente cyte wel garnysshyd named albane iourneyes fro anthyoche assyeged constreyned within yelded toun te hym entred therin helde moyen therof prysoners sansadol gaf hym grete good rychesse wherfor delyuerd bothe lady childeren sayson cam grete plente peple ducheland arryued e port seynt syme soiournd within anthyoche mortalyte endured yet suche wyse deyde almost alle ther escaped alle deed short tyme ffor pestylence continued thre monethes hool vnto thentree wynter deed knyghtes vc mene peple noman knewe nombre peple retorned anthyoche strong wel garnysshyd ffro albare taken viij myle noman myght holde l nger theyr comyn peple desirous goo iherusalem atte daye named alle redy therle tholouse duc godeffroye eustace broder therle fflaundres duc normandye tancre cam cyte mar assieged toun moch rych ful grete pryde specially cause yere assemblee scarmoche ayenst oure men whome toke somme somme slewe suche wyse better ffor cause preysed lasse pylgryms blamed iniuryed baron despyted alle thoost beyng walles vpon hye towres sette vp cross spytte despyt fayth made shameful thynges angre oure peple baron moche wroth dyde crye assault assailled toun asprely suche wyse yf laddres th wolde haue entred cyte force ij daye cam theder thyrde day cam buymont whiche brought men hym largely lodged cyte assieged thenne men grete despyte dyde nothyng hastely dyde make engyns reysed castellys belfroyes slynges caste stone fylled dyches goo vnder myne walles within deffended moche wel threwe vpon grete stone fyre brent lyme oyle boyllyng shotte arbalasters bowe turquoys arowes passyng thycke god thaked hurted fewe oure men within began moche wery r men apperceyued theyr volente hardynesse grewe encreaced anon dressyd laddres ayenst walles wente vp dylygently emong alle ther noble valyaut man limosyn named geffrey de tour mayntened fyrst tyme merueyllously well folowed hym th r ynowe entred toures taken cyte yf nyght come destroubled therfore ey left til morn ffor assault edured fro sone rysyng tyl tyme kept wel gate toun shold yssue made good watche thooste men peple sawe none shewde hym vpon th walles entred toun fonde voyde peple ke alle wolde nede longe fred famyne grete pouerte alle cyte entred longe caues depe supposed haue saued k pt morn baron sawe cyte tak n entred founde lytil gayne ffor comyn eple taken suche founde knewe wel ur kes toun hyd vnder erthe sette fyre mowthes alle caues sente moche smoke force muste come oure men slewe ynowgh remenaunt toke prysonners deyde sekenesse good man holy relygyous whiche moche louyd dredde oure lord god guyllame bisshop orenge whan duc abyden xv dayes departed le fflaundres cam anthyoche duc godeffroy wold goo rage vysyte brother er began way iherusalem somme aduentures cao cliiij godeffroy valyaunt duc loreyne sawe men fote made redy taccomplysshe theyr vowe goo towarde iherusalem moche requyred admones ed grete lordes valyaunt duc wold see vysyte brother fore shold departe fro countr toke pryne companye wente rage whan seen broder doo suche thynges plesyth hym wold retorne anthyoche baron pylgryms abode hym whan approuched six seuen myle ryde founde theyr waye moche fayre place dyne ete fayre welle moche delectable ful grete herbes grasse alle acorded gladly dyne fayr place whyles made redy theyr dyner ye certayn oute moche reed whiche nyghe mareys aroos certayn turkes wel armed whan noble duc baron sawe come toke theyr armes hastely myght toke theyr horse ran vpon vygorously skarmoche grete fiers duc dyde moche wel valyauntly ther many turkes slayn remenaut fledde men lost nothyng cam moche grete ioye vnto anthyoche cyte albare conquerd grete debate aroos btywene therle tholouse buymont cao clv noble cyte albare taken haue sayd fore aroos grete debate bytwene buymont erle tholouse ffor therle wold haue alle albare buymont sayde wold gyue away part yf yelded gaf ouer certeyn towres held anthyoche herupon buymont departed made towres assaylled men erles tholouse helde toke strength made goo kept name therle fro forthon helde alle anthyoche withoute felaw partener therle sawe buymont departed fro cyte conquerd gaf toun entierly bisshop albare whyles ordeyned disposed bytwene hym bisshop cyte myght mayntened kept suche wyse turkes shold recouer peple foote began murmure hye noble men taryed take euyl cytees made debate noyse emong theyr conquest pryncipal cause wherfor departed fro theyr coutrees lefte forgetyng settyng therby semed sette nothynge thaccomplysshyng theyr vowe therfor mene peple acorded emonge self sone therle tholouse shold departed fro cyte marran shold confounde destroye alle vnto erthe suche wyse wold tarye hym fro forthon happed baron assembled rouge cyte whiche half waye bytwene marran anthyoche ffor haue counseyl emonge yf shold fro then drawe forth toward iherusalem ffor ne peple languysshyd moche hasted goo theder baron coude acorde conclusion taken whyles therle tholouse abode parlement foote men lefte marran ayenst wyll deffence bisshop bete doun walles toures cyte marran ffor wold thoccasion toun abide lenger countre whan erle retorned moche angry coude amende couerd well courage withoute forth men foote began alway requyre moche baron wold conduyte taccomplysshe theyr pylgremage yf wold wold chese knyght make hym capytayn ouer shold folowe hym vnto cyte iherusalem syde grete scarsete thoost vytaylles wyse poure peple deyde honger men sayde many flesshe men thynges fayr n good ne honeste ete herof sourded grete mortalyte ffor holden siege cyte marran suche schy famyne lost moche theyr peple many armes mesease suffred ther deyde moch noble valyaunt yonge man emorran sone huon erle seynt poul sekenesse wa grete dommage moch bewaylled thoost atte request comyn peple erle tholouse ordeyned day conduyte cao clvj thyse inconuenientes ran thoost pilgryms vygorous valyaunt erle tholouse moch grete anguysshe ffor wyste wel myght doo one syde pyte grete sorowe meseases sawe poure peple suffre moche meuyd theyr requestes whan swetly prayd hym baron lede taccomplysshe theyr vowes pylgremage taken fynde therin ledde away horse ynow whiche founde pasture emong men dyuerse messagers contre grete lordes men ther aboutes sente see theyr couyne whiche whan sawe oure baron dyde thus theyr wylle nothynge myght resiste wente theyr lordes told ouer cruel fiers peple aspre hardy thennne shold ye haue seen brought presented oure men grete presentes honorable vytaylles nought fro alle partes moche doubted dyde grete cure tacqueynte brynge theyr loue longe passed alle contre til cam playnes auncyent cyte see syde named archys lodged nygh toun therle tholouse approuched hoost vnto archis situacion cao clviijo arrhys cyte lande fenyce standeth atte foote montayne named lybane tereitorye moche stronge four v myle fro see hath moche plenteuous londe aboute delectable pasture water scripture saye founded moche auncyently arke iij sone one named caym sone named canaham hym cam sone arracheus founded cyte hym cyte named archys ther prisonners oure men toun hit sente worde tho prysonners therle tholouse shold assiege cyte also baron ffor shold haue grete good therby cite tripl moch noble rych vj myle thes ther also peple prysonners syth begynnynge siege anthyoche goten peple began renne contree nycely folyly seche somme vytaylles necessitees lacked taken many place wyse ther vnneth cyte ne castel contre ther therin som pylgryms prysoners cyte trypple moo ij c self sente oure men yf wolde make semblaunt conquere countree kyng trypple wold gyue grete hauoyr good depart then shold delyuer alle theyr prysonners happeed thene thus peple approuched cyte archis see semblaunt wold make also tabyde baron shortly shold come folowe toun named tortuose whiche raymont toke rowte pylgryms departynge baron fro anthyoche capitulo clixo ther yssued lodgys oure men honderd men horsbak two honderd foote made theyr capytayne raymont pelet whiche wyseman moche valyaunt knyght wente fore cyte whiche named tortuose see yf myght fynde ony auenture gete som gayne approuched cyte began tassayle vygorously moche sharply within deffended bothe men wymme valiautly men left litil nought nyght cam left thassault feessh morn abode companye thooste shold folowe begyn morn thassault agayn toun moch grete drede wold assaille agayn morn myght resiste therfor nyght wente pryuely toun wente montaines caryed nothyng theyr wyues childeren theyr geer lefte toun oure men knewe thynge herof aroos erly began make redy encorage eche doo wel thassault approched walles alle armed herde noman entred toun opened yates wyse alle entred thenne sawe toun yssued goon founde cyte ful goodes moche alle ryche trussed bare moche myght thoost recounted theyr aduenture whiche alle glad ioyous thanked lord whan moneth marche come season attemperat people left anthyoche sawe tyme departe spak duc godeffroy therle fflaundres prayed moche affectuously wold enterpryse coduice ih lm taccomplysshe pilgremage goyng forth therle tholouse duc normandye cancre caused moche haue wyll forth ffor goon fore ledde grete nombre pylgryms happened wel waye therby grete prouffyte grete honour thyse wordes baron gretely stered meuyd ordeyned theyr affayres dylygently toke alle theyr peple wel horsbak foote wente fer f rth cam lyche surrye xxvm men poynt armed eueryche wa good man valyaunt knyght buymont conueyed theder men theyr entente ne wyll shold goo ony ferther ffor cyte anthyoche newly conquerd theyr enemyes fast therfor behoued hym withdrawe hym ferre fro therfor toke good hede continuelly daye nyght grete courage conueyed theder toke leue wepte moche departyng recoauded god retorned agayn anthyoche hoost abode lyche moche auncyent cyte noble stondeth vpon ryuage see cyte surye theperour constantinoble lord longe fore er oure men cam theder comen guyneuyers spak long fore born boloyne vpon see syde arryued tharse whyles bawd wyn broder duc helde comen lyche shippe supposed haue taken toun force folysshly conteyned hym assaylled toun yssued lyghtly toke hym yet helde hym pryson whan onre baron cam theder duc knewe born londe fadre ben companye therle bawdwyn brother therfor demaunded hym grete men toun prayde entierly wold delyuere hym durst gayne saye hym delyuerd hym felawship shippe duc commaunded hym shold goo see alwaye coosteyeng hooste dyde gladly saylled forth duc assieged gybelet trayson whiche lefte siege cao clxo hoost departed fro lyche whan oure baron receyued theyr prysonners late departed f cylyce fro anthyoche fro cytres aboute alle comen arryued theder suche wyse alle wente gydre see syde vnto cyte named gybelet whiche fro lyche xij myle abode assieged cyte baylly calyphe egypte helde cyte see side vnder power calyphe egypte baylle yssued saufcoduyt spak duc godefroy offred vjm besauntes many grete yeftes aboue departe reyse siege fro then duc wold wyse moche swetly expresly wold leue theyr siege come dylygently hym suche wyse myght alle gydre whan peple cam whan duc othe baron herde thynge moche anguysshous meuyd ffor supposed certaynly alle trewe anon departed fro gybelet cyte valerne wente whiche aboue castel margat syth cam marche whiche first cyte londe fenyce whan wente toward northeest fro then cam cyte cortuose isle somtyme cyte abode shippes theyr naure wote many dayes hasted cam fore cyte archys tancre yssued oute thoost cam enst tolde alle longe tromperye barat therle tholouse moche angry therfore lodged part fro doo broken theyr syege erle knewe loue baron newe comen therfor sent messagers sayde name moche fayre w rdes brought grete yeftes wherfore short tyme happed alle repeased amyable good frendes gydre sauf tancre whiche acorded hym accused hym many thynges fore comynge thise laste baros peple therles tholouse myght nothynge auaylle prouffyte ayenst cyte whiche assieged grete hope shold soon brought ende accomplysshyd thayde newe come neuertheles fyll supposed ffor alle tymes contryued ony engyne tassaylle walles alway fyll contrarye purposed toun brake alle theyr ouurages suche wyse loste costes payne appered wel lord withdrawen fro ayde good wyll within toun slewe many without deyde tweyne noble valyaunt knyghtes wete ancean ribemont alway dyde valyauntly sommeuer cam potom de baladon hye man wel acqueynted therle tholouse siege displesyd ouer moche alle thooste especial footemen whiche moche grete desyre taccomplysshe theyr vowe iherusalem also whan duc comen ben fore began withdrawe fro werke suche wyse euery man dyde nought ffor plesyd wel therle greued ennoyed myght departe lede forth baron thoost murmured spere founden anthyoche grete myracle happed presence alle hoste capitulo clxjo renewed word whiche comyn people also baron whiche began doubte spere founden anthyoche lyke ye haue herde fore ffor somme sayde certaynly spere opened syde oure lord crosse precious blood bydewed reuelacion oure lord founden holy good man recomforte people whiche grete necessyte nede sayde fals tromperye abuse ffor therle tholouse fonden contryued mene peple drawe gete syluer theyr offrynges altercacion meuyd preest named arnold chppellayn moche acqueynted noble duc normandye wel lettred good lyf ouer malycious pourchassoure discordes ye shal afterward book rumour grete thoost haue sayd man fonde spere herde doubte peple cam fore baron moche hardily sayd maner fayr lordes doubte ye nothyng werke hath ben barat n tromperye theryn hath none comen god certaynly comfort cristen peple ynte andrew appered wylle saueour ihesu crist whiche deuysed alle maner haue founden shewe yow saye trouth praye ye make grete fyre merueyllous shal entre holde spere hand shal passe goo thurgh hool sauf whan herd acorded alle therto fyre made brennyd lyght greete merueyllous blessyd good fryday plesed thynge shold thus p euyd day lord smeton herte spere thus fred hym self thus enterprysed preue named peter bertilme clerk litil lettred coude vnderstonde without forth moche symple man ne alle thooste assembled aboute fyre peter cam forth kneled doun recommande hym vnto god whan made prayer toke spere entred fyre passed thurgh nothynge hym perysshed n hur e ony man coude see knowe whan peple sawe alle ranne kysse hym made hym moche grete ioye doubte thenne wende veryly quenchid yet sourded gretter errour murmur fore ffor longe clerke deyde thenne sayde somme thanguysshe fyre toke deth shold thoccasion therof sayde yssued oute al hool sauf fro fyre wylle lord syth trouthe knowen shold deye thus peraduenture prees cam vpon hym grete whan yssued ou fyre therby hurte maner murmured yet peple emong thamabassade egipte com n men thooste pylgryms reuerence cao c lxijo somme messagiers sente egypte baron atte requeste cam vnto anthyoche fro calyphe egypte reteyned holden force barat wel yere retourned comen messagers calyphe brought baron fro hym wordes moche dyuerse moch chauged fro sente fore anthyoche ffor thenne sente shold conteyne vygorously ayenst sowdan perse shold haue hym grete ayde gold syluer vytaylles chaunged moche langage ffor sente worde thought dyde moch grete thyng yf suffred pilgrim myght goo iherusalem ij c gydre iij c alle vnarmed whan made theyr prayer theyr pylgremage retorne saufly agayn whan oure baron herd herof grete desdayne sayde messagers shold retorne agayn theyr lord telle hym licence ne leue wold goo iherusalem vnarmed one another shold goo maulgre hym alle gydre bataylles renged baners reysed desployed shal say calyphe egypte reysen grete pryde whan men discomfyted corbagat fore anthyoche power soudan perse moche affebled wise none neyghbours doubted hym ne fered make warre agaynst hym ffor alwaye werse whiche occasion happed conestable calyphes egypte named emites taken cyte iherusalem fro men soudan perse whiche holden xxxviij yere therfore sawe nowe calyphe aboue disconfyture men corbagat wende shold haue nede ony ayde therfor despysed peple ambassade fro themperour constantinoble comen pylgryms thanswer sayd ambassade ca clxiijo syde comen messagers fro themperour constantinoble whiche couerd thenne sente hastely messagers iherusalem vnto baron abode awayted certaynte thynge bad hastely come alle sauf suche shold kepe cyte shold brynge alle peple moche hastely fyghte ayenst grete plente theyr enemyes men assembled ordeyned theyr bataylles fyghte ayenst turkes turkes discon yted capitulo ccijo therle tholouse baron hym knewe certaynte theyr enemyes cam vpon grete power therfor gadred gydre alle theyr men iherusalem yssued come moch dilygently playnes duc atte place named elyn whan alle assembled nombred theyr peple fonde xijc horsmen footemen ix whan thoost men ben one day therabout euen songe whan hegan wexe derk espyed fer greet prees cam takyng vp coutrey couerd grete partes playnes oure men supposed certaynly thoost sarasyns merueylled moche cam ayenst hour thenne sente oute ijc horsmen armed lightly wel horsed see nygh peple cam many roode forth good paas whan approuched knewe ox kyen mare ther many semed moo alle world myght suffyse alle peple ther thyse beestes comen men horsbak whiche kepte theuys commaunded herdmen shold doo sente forth baron retorned sayde ther none beestes thenne alle oure men ran theder kepars fledde myght somme ther taken whiche tolde trouthe turkes suche wyse wel knowen grete hooste sarasyns lodged vij myle purpoos come ee alle baron thenne certayn bataylle deuysed emonge ix bataylles commaunded thre shold goo fore one syde playnes greet thir shold goo mydle thre shold come behynde samsyns myght noman knowe nombre ffor ther grete plen e euery daye encreaced grewe contre whiche ranne suche wyse estemed whan men goten grete gayne spak saye alle beestes grete ioye ioyously reseyd nyght charge made good watche vpon thooste morn whan sonne rysen duc dyde crye euery man shold arme hym goo bataylle wente forth soft paas right theder thought fynde theyr enemyes stedfaste hope lord lyght thynge make lasse nombre vaynquysshe gretter egypte mescreautes cam moche grete desraye vnto place sawe oure peple alle playne whan sawe knewe men noo talente withdrawe ne eschewe cam seche began moche doubte whan sawe oure men taken pourprised grete place playns wel supposed ben mochemore people greter nombre trouthe suche h ue sayd men fewe horsbak foote g te company beestes haue sayd whan ey drewe forth beestes wente turkes de ben alle men armed ouer grete fere drede grettest men men supposed shold best haue born fayte bataylle began withdrawe lytil lytil lefte theyr bataylles one fledde pryuely whan lasse knyghtes turkmans apperceyued neuer toke hope torned horse smote spore fledde euery man supposed best saue hym daye lost sette al herte sowe pourchasse discordes ouer al byleuyd noman wote wher becam bisshop maturane somme men sayde duc sente hym fetche baron left cyte whan retorned sarasins shold haue take hym slayn hym brought hym pryson sommeuer cam hym grete harme effaced holy company whan oure baron sawe lord foghten put hertes turkes grete fere drede fled without smytynge stroke grete ioye rendred grace thankynges oure lord deuoutly counseyl shold f lowe withoute raye thurgh feldes ffor ouer grete nombre peple vnto regarde yf happed relye gadre gydre agayn myght perauenture put oure men werse oure men rode alle ordenauce vnto tentes hethen men ffor fledde loked neuer behynde founde oure men grete plente gold syluer robe iewellys vessell leest ynowgh thus gadred alle fonde retorned wente agayn iherusalem euery man laden charged despoylles thankyng preysing lord comen vyctorye honour gayne thenne made within cyte moche ioye grete doon vaynquers conquerours whan departe theyr gayne somme baron wolde retorne home theyr pylgremage cao cciijo maner conteyned cyte iherusalem two valyaunt men ben longe tyme seruyse lord perfourmed theyr pylgremage wyte duc normandye therle fflaunders toke leue baron toke theyr waye retorne theyr countrey cam shippe constantinople themperour alexys seen fore receyued moche fayr chiere gaf moche fayre yeftes theyr de artyng cam theyr countre hool ioyous one duc normandye founde thynge alle chaunged otherwyse countre lefte ffor whyles mayntenyng holy pylgremage lyke ye haue herd oldest broder deyde without heyer body wylliam rous whiche kyng englond right customes countre royamme fallen duc normandye broder whiche yonger named henry cam baron countrey made vnderstande tha duc broder kyng iherusalem talente ne purposed neuer retorne syde montaynes lesynge made hym kynge englond becam men whan broder retorned fro holy londe demaunded hym herytage entierly wold delyuer hym duc made redy grete nauye gadryd moche peple myght normandye place passed se arryued force broder kynge cam ayens hym alle power lande bat ylles al redy tassemble noble wysemen sawe shold ouer grete hurt damage yf thyse two bretheren shold fyght thus therfor spak pe made manere sayd henry shold holde royamme sholde gyue euery yere brother greet somme good whiche made hym sure thus retorned duc agayn cam londe happed kyng whiche somme castellys normandye fore royamme englond wolde kepe herytage duc demaunded wold delyue thenne duc assieged toke force whan kyng herd moche angry assemblid grete peple passed ouer normandye brother cam ayenst hym fought gydre tynche bray ther duc disconfyted taken broder put hym pryson wherin deyde thenne henry alle gydre royamme englond duchye normandye therle tholouse cam vnto yche surye lefte wyf countesse wente vnto constantynople shold hastely retorne themperour made hym grete ioye receyued hym moche wel gaf hym grete yeftes cam agayn wyf hoole sauf felawship surye two yere ye shal duc godeffroy iherusalem wel gouerned royamme whiche oure lord gyuen hym reteyned hym erle garnyer grece baron suche myght haue tancre valyaunt abode hym duc gaf holde herytage cyte tabarye whiche stondeth laye geme alle pryncipalyte galylee cyte whiche woned named porphire nowe named cayphas alle thappertenaunces thyse thynges tancre helde thyse londes wel wysely alowed god honoured world fouded chirches countrey moche rychely gaf grete rente endowed aournementes fayr grete valure specially chirche nazareth tabarye mount tabor lefte hye estate moche ryche poynt baron hym haue lordes countrey haue taken ynowgh tenours tancre wyse trewe delyted hym doo wel chirches appereth whan prynce anthyoche ffor enhaunced chirche seynt peter pryncipalyte seygnorye athyoche made moch tecrece enlarged ye shal buymont bawdwyn beyng certayn pryse conqueste iherusalem wolde accomplysshe theyr pylgremage capitulo cciiijo whyles royamme iherusalem estate buymont prynce anthyoche bawdwyn erle rage broder duc godeffroy herd certayn tydynges baron helde gydre bretheren accompanye theyr pylgremage thayde helpe lord ihesu criste conquerd vpon turkes recouerd oure fayth holy cyte iherusalem whiche accomplysshyd theyr vowes theyr pylgremages therfor assembled day named goo holy sepulc e thende assaylled theyr vowes desired moche see duc baron wold gyue ayde yf nede wete bodyes theyr goodes theyr men vnder thyse two hye men takynge holy cyte iherusalem ffor wylle pylgryms one abode anthyoche rage kepe soygnously defende turkes fro thyse two cytees whiche fer fro cristiente eche man doo ynowgh countrey lefte alle come buymont cam fyrst fro cyte moche fayr company grete nombre men armes horsbak foote cam vnto cyte vpon e named valerne castel margat lodged hym maulgre cyte bawdwyn cam fro countrey sone moch iourneied ouertoke prynce buymont fore cyte assembled tyme arryued pylgryms ytalye lyche surye emong good man wyse wel lettred relygyous grete honneste named daybart archebisshop pyse another company archebysshop puylle cyte named acian thyse men theyr meyne cam companye thyse two baron passe surely vnto cyte iherusalem moche encreced thoost thyse two prynces suche wyse wel xxv horsbak foote thus thenne helde theyr waye suche maner fonde cyte theyr enemyes wherfore passed moch grete payne suffred moche theyr way lack vytaylles ffor fonde none hy suche brought fro theyr countrey faylled ha e grete cold grete rayne nothyng myght endure ueylous moneth iuyll whiche moche rayny customably countrey ffor cause many deyed esease companye ffor alle longe waye myght fynde none wold selle ony vytaylle sauf tryple cesaire grete sarce e vytaylles theyr horse atte laste mercy lord cam iherusalem receyued moche grete ioye god baron clergye alle peple vysyted holy place cyte te ri grete sorowes herte fylle doun flat stratched chirches kyssed ete therthe lord bought cam theyr hostel lys alle toun made grete ioye whan hye feste natyuyte lord ihesu criste approuched alle prelate baron yssued iherusalem wente bethlehem helde theyr cristemas behelde gladly moche ententyfly holy crybbe wherin sauyour world laye bytwene beestes deuoutly made theyr prayer orysons place whiche lytil dyche swete lady moder vyrgyne chylded wrapped sone lytil smale clothys gaf hym souke mylke pappes cristen men chosen patriarke iherusalem assigned hym rente cao ccvo vn tyme see iherusalem ben without pastour patriark duely truly entred wel thene v monethes cyte conquerd thenne assembled baron counseylle haue suche man worthy honour myght bere faytes ther wordes ynowgh somme wolde haue one wold haue another atte laste counseyl good wyll alle chees daybart archibisshop pyse whiche newly come constituted sette hym siege patriark ffor made baratour arnold haue spoken fore lyke made ayenst right reson lyke wyse retorned agayn nought whan good wyse man sette dignyte duc godeffroy prynce buymont cam fore hym whiche gyuen hym honour vycayre ihesu criste londe thanked preysed alle gydre oure lord whan assygned rente newe patriark suche predecessour whiche greeke holden gretter aboue suche wyse myght honorably mayntene good honest company peple thenne bawdwyn buymont toke leue duc baron descended vnto flom iordan bayned ffro then wente ryuer syde til cam tabarye thenne passed londe named fenyce lefte cesayre right syde cam cyte named manbec helde see syde moche exployted cam al hool sound anchy c e thatysement somme men grete debate sour ed bytwene duc patriarke iherusalem cao ccvjo customme somme men suche may suffre pea emong peple may set e scorde thatysement suche maner folke sourded debate bytwene duc patriarke ffor patriarke demau ded hym chyef tour toun whiche named dauyd fourth part iherusalem aboue wold haue cyte iaphe alle thappertenauntes ffor e sayde dr ytes rightes chirche sepulcre whan debate whyle endured bytwene duc whiche humble mesurable moche doubted lord candelmas day presence alle clergye peple gaf iiij part iaphe moche debonayrly patriarke chirche holde euermore whan cam day eester fore assembled feste gaf honde patriark fourth part iherusale tour dauyd alle appertenauntes alway forseen couenaunt due shold holde thyse cytees londes aboute vnto tyme ayde oure lord conquerd vpon turkes two cytees whiche royame myght enlarged yf happed deyde mene whyle without h yer alle thyse thynges withoute diction shold come honde patriarke chirche trouthe suche haue sayd ouer grete merueylle ffor reson holy man wyse dema ded thus thyse cytees noble man duc haue sayd knewe state londe helde reputed self lasse whan vnderstode werke couetyse chirche merueylled therof ffor baron conquerd cyte gaf duc frely wold ony man lyuyng shold haue right aboue hym shold holde hym self entierly without making ony ony obeyssaunce hier recounteth thystorye fourth parte iherusalem cam vnto patriarke cao ccvijo alway certayn fro tyme latin entred cyte yet auncyente patriarke iherusalem fourth part cyte iherusalem helde owen happed reson shal saye shortly ffor trouthe therof hath ben serched founden thauncyent historyes whyles cyte hondes hethen peple myght neuer haue pea longe endured ofte assieged hethen prynces ffor eche wold conquere put seygnorye therfor toke ofte proyes mesdyde trespaced cytezeyns toun brake towres walles moche oultrageously theyr engyns oldenes walles cyte disclosed open many place tyme royamme egypte ryche puyssaut hauoyr good defence ony royammes turkye ffor calyphe helde thenne iherusalem londe therabout grete hoost sente theder conquerd alle surye vnto lyche whiche anthyoche thus encreced empyre establysshyd bayllyes cytees stonde see syde londe thenne commanded alle sholde paye hym trybute ordeyned deuysed wold haue euery cyte wold cytezeyns shold make agayn wallis eu cyte mayntene good poynt towres redresse alle aboute suche neded aduys men theyr establysshement bayly iherusalem commaunded toun repayre theyr walles sette entierly poynt lyke fore ben thenne ordeyned deuysed moch euery strete toun shold make grete cruelte malyce commaunded caytyfs cristiens cyte shold make fourth part walles pour greued tayllages excise vnnethe emong alle wherof repayre two wrettys sawe wel sought occasion destroye alle therfore assembled cam moche humbly fore bayly fy foot moch requyred weping wold commande doo thynge myght doo ffor h commaunded doo ouermoche ouer theyr rewe inhumayn baylly whiche ful cruelte pryde bouyd cristen men menaced moche f e sly sware yf accompl sshyd commaundement lord calyphe wold smyte theyr heedes tra tour whan herd moche aferd othersyde sawe wel myght bere charge leyde therfor dyde moche e laste prayer somme turkes whiche pyte baylly gaf respyte til sent themperour constantynople requyre hym loue god wold sende almesse performe horrible werke delyuer fro peryll deth whiche condempned yf made mater cao ccvii messagers cam fro themperou constantynople seyd hym trouth message subiection meseases fylthes turkes hard withstondyng muste essaye ffor myght passe none maner sente good messagers trewe grete lord calyphe egypte lord helpe hym wyse thei fode hym sought shortly say delyuerd good chartre sealid seal
