themperour lyke commaunded werke made yere thyncarcion oure lord mlxiij thenne calyphe kynge egypte bommensor xxxvj yere fore cyte conquerd vnto tyme cristen men lodged toun emonge turkes comynly one another fro then forth calyphe commauded fourth part toun delyuerd thenne cristen men moche eased ffor whan dwellyd emong turkes theyr neyghbours dyde grete ennoyes shame whan self dyde moche yf ony debate emonge self brought fore patriark ffor fro thene forth part toun none iustice thus gouned oune iiij part bouded shall saye ffro yate yt sone goth doun named yate dauid tour angle otherwyse named tour tancre walles made within bounded fro chyef way goth fro gate vnto chaunge fro then agayn vnto west yate space stondeth mount caluarye sauyour ihesu criste crucified holy sepulcre laye deed wherof aroos fro deth lyf hows hospytal two abbayes one monkes another nonnes hows patriarke cloysture chanonnes sepulcre duc godeffcoy augmente cristiente assieged one townes turkes cao ccixo tyme alle baron come pylgremage departed fro londe retorned theyr countrees valyaunt duc royamme delyud tancre whiche abiden hym almost allone tho partes moche pour good men vnnethe myght make whan dyde alle theyr power thre honderd men horsbak two thousand foote cyttes pylgryms conquerd ferre sondre none myght come without grete peryll theyr enemyes vyllages cytees whiche called casians therin dwellyd turkes theyr subgettis obeyed lordes cytees thise turk hated nome han dyde cristen men pourchaced incessantly alle harme euyl myght whan fonde ony men allone way gladly murdred somtyme ledde cytees sarasyns selle yet thought gretter meschyef folye ffor wold ere ne laboure theyr londes thede lordes men cytees shold take theyr rente desired self lyuer suffre mesease rather peple shold haue ony good auaylle cristen men well assured within cytees ffor fewe people cam theuys nyght robbed theyr house slewe theyr beddes bare awaye alle theyr thynges occasion many cristen men lefte theyr fayr tenementes howses cytees retourned pryuely theyr countreyes ffor hadde grete drede turkes whiche dwellyd aboute sholde assemble somme daye take townes strengthe destresse destroye euer wyse neuer sholde memorye ffor hate fyrst londe hat nement londe shold cause ther many alle theyr thynges fled away better assured cam agayn lawe thus neuer herd whyles royamme thus poue te valyaunt duc godeffroy moche gret good hope lord enlarged hi royamme assembled moche peple myght wente tassiege cyte nygh iaph see syde named arsur fonde wel garnysshed vytaylles men armes engyns ther therin turkes many hardy defensable hoost cristen men withoute fewe suffretous cause shippes whiche myght defende waye see myght entre yssue whan plesyd ffor thise thynges duc constrayned leue siege departed thynkyng come agayn place whan tyme shold couenable better pourueyed men wherof nede take toun yf lord gyuen hym long lyf world turkes brought presentes duc godeffroy sayd siege theyr deuyses gydre cao ccxo happed siege whiche haue spoken thynge ought forgoten ffro montaynes londe samarye whiche londe napples cam summe turkes whiche lordes casians theraboute brought vnto valyaunt duc godeffroy presentes brede wyn date fruyte myght wel cam te pye beyng contenaunce men thynge prayde moch men duc brought fore hym thenne presented hym suche brought noble duc humble without hobaunc sat pauyllon lened vnto sak full stuff abode part sente fourage whan made sawe duc sytte lowe merueylled th peple vnderstode theyr hye prynce te slayn many saunt royamme cont yned hym tappytys ne clothes hym ne aboute hym sergean naked swerdes haches axis sawe hym shold doubte fere hym satt lytil affayre valiaut duc demauded knewe vnderstode theyr langage sayde told answerd merueylled thenne sayd shame man mortel sytte vpon therthe ffor theder muste retorne deth lodge body become erthe whan herd answere comen te pye essaye began moche allowe preyse wytte humilyte departed fro then sayeng shapen lyke lord alle londe gouerne peple withoute pryde knewe pouerte fragilyte nature wel word spr dd ouer al herd hym moche deadde doubted enemyes enquyred affayres whiche founde hym vygour rayson mesure without ony pryde oultrage buymont taken goyng meletene whiche cyte lord wold yelde hym cao ccxjo royamme iherusalem conteyned thus ye haue herd thenne happened ryche man e menye named gabryel lord cyte meletene stondeth yonde ryuer eufrates londe meso tayne gabriel doubted moche turkes perse shold ome hym ffor men helde ran ofte hym suche wyse myght wel suffre therfore toke counseyl sente messag buymont prynce anthyoche shold saye name shold haste hym londe ffor ouer hym cyte certayn couenauntes whiche sente hym lo yd buymont leuer buymont cyte turkes sholde take hym ayenst wyll whan herde thyse tydynges hardy hasted oche make hym redy toke hym good company went forth way passed ryuer euf entred mesopotayne nyghe cyte meletene ffor whiche wente receyue whan puyssaunt amyral turkes named domsmayn certaynly ry knowleche comynge laye awayte hym ranne vpon hym sodenly men beyng alle arraye dispourueyed abode alle slayn ffor ther er grete plente turkes fledde buymont taken reteyned ladde hym handes bounden cordes foot chayned wyth yron auenture mounted turke grete pryde rusted moche hoost ledde cam fore cyte meletene assieged cause supposed wold haue delyuerd without taryeng somme escaped fro then prynce taken cam fleyng cyte rage told therle bawdwyn grete mesauenture fallen whan valyaunt erle herd moche angrye grete pyte prynce helde broder companye pylgremage cause theyr countrees nygh gydre shold haue displesyd hym yf turkes shold conquere cyte buymont shold haue therfor somoned hastely alle men myght haue horsbak fote toke hym necessarye suche vyage wente toward thoo partyes wel thre daye iourneye rage fro meletene sone passed waye suchewyse nyghe cyte sayd donysmayn knewe wel comyng therle durst abyde ne fyght hym lefte siege departed ledde forth hym buymont faste bounden straytly whan bawdwyn herde durst abyde hym fledde fore hym ran men chaced hym thre dayes longe whan sawe myght ouertake hym retourned cyte meletene gabryel lord toun receyued hym moche grete ioye alle men made good chere gaf ouer cyte hym couenauntes offred buymont whan reborned home agayn rage duc godeffroy assembled alle peple entred arabye gayn made deth capitulo ccxijo godeffroy valyaunt duc men lefte hym kepe royamme began haue moche grete mesease suffre suche pouerte vnnethe may deuysed thenne happed good espyes trewe brought hym tidynges partyes arabye syde f om iordan moche ryche peple whiche doubted nothynge therfore dwellyd fortress yf surprised shold moch grete gayne wonne valyaunt duc moche suffred toke hym peple foote horsbak many myght sauf garde cyte thenne entred sodeynly londe enemyes gadred many grete proyes wete horse beufes yen sheep ryche prysonners brought grete plente thenne retorned toward iherusalem somme turkes ther hye purssaunt arabye whiche moche hardy noble armes grete pry emonge ther one longe desired see duc godeffroye boloyne wold fayn knowe yf trewe said force stregthe acqueynte hym peple ffraunce herd moche come fro occident vnto th yent conquerd many londes sette theyr subiection aboue alle desired see duc godeffroy knowe yf trouth sayd prowesse strengthe dide moch spak good sure trie w come vnto duc salewed hym moche lowe enclynyng lyke theyr customme prayd desired duc moche humbly wold plese hym smyte swerd camel brought moche grete ffor sayde shold grete honour hym countre yf myght recounte ony stroke seen hym self duc knewe wel come fro see hym dyde requyred hym drewe swerd smote camel neck grettest smote lyghtly ben sheep whan turke sawe merueylled ouer moche wyse abasshed whan litil thought hym sayd langage see wel sayd duc hath good swerd wel trenchant cuttyng wote neuer yf coude smyte grete strook another swerde valyaunt duc demaunded sayde whan knewe began smyle lytil sayd shold delyuer hym owen swerde turke dyde duc thenne smote therwith camel suche wyse made hede flee moche lyghtlyer thenne merueylled ouer moche turk sayde strengthe arme bounte swerd wel preuyd trewe sayd duc countreye thenne gaf duc many fayr iewellys gold ryche stone moche acqueynted hym retorned home countre valyaunt duc cam vnto iherusalem alle proye truss fardellys gayn wer grete men companye ryche moneth iuyll velyaunt duc godefroy whiche gouernour royamme iherusalem maladye sekenes moch grete alle phisiciens contre sente dyde alle possible alle auaylled ffor payne encresyd alway sente men relygyon prelate curate good deuoute men haue couseyll helthe sowle moche wel confessyd veray repentaunt grete wepynges right mynde grete deuocion departed world certaynly ought thynke sowle brought vp angelis fore face ihesu crist deyde xiij day iuyll yere thyncaruacion oure lord j c entiered buryed chirche holy sepulcre vnder place mount caluarye lord put crosse place kept moche honestly entere burye kynges vnto day thus endeth book intitled laste siege conquest iherusalem many historyes therin comprysed fyrst eracles meseases cristen men holy londe releef conquest iherusalem godeffroy boloyne first kyng latyns royamme deth translated reduced ffreusshe englysshe symple persone wylliam caxton thende euery cristen man may better encoraged tenterprise warre defense cristendom recouer sayd cyte iherusalem whiche oure blessyd sauyour ihesu criste suffred deth al mankynde roose fro deth lyf fro holy londe ascended heuen also cristen peple one vnyed veray pea myght empryse goo theder pylgremage strong honde expelle sarasyns turkes lord myght ther seruyd worshipped chosen cristen peple holy blessyd londe incarnate blissyd presence blessyd body whyles erthe emonge v whiche conquest myght deserue present short transitorye lyf celestial lyf dwelle heuen eternally ioye without ende amen book presente vnto mooste cristen kynge kynge edward fourth humbly besechyng hyenes take displesyr presumyng whiche boook began marche xij daye fynysshyd vij day iuyn yere lord mcccclxxxj xxj yere regne sayd sauerayn lord kyng edward fourth maner sette forme enprynted xx day nouembre yere forsayd thabbay westmester sayd wylliam caxton
